← all editions

Sophocles' Ajax

Geoffrey Steadman

Ἀθ
1ἀεὶ μέν, ὦ παῖ Λαρτίου, δέδορκά σε
2πεῖράν τιν᾽ ἐχθρῶν ἁρπάσαι θηρώμενον·
3καὶ νῦν ἐπὶ σκηναῖς σε ναυτικαῖς ὁρῶ
4Αἴαντος, ἔνθα τάξιν ἐσχάτην ἔχει,
5πάλαι κυνηγετοῦντα καὶ μετρούμενον
6ἴχνη τὰ κείνου νεοχάραχθ᾽, ὅπως ἴδῃς
7εἴτ᾽ ἔνδον εἴτ᾽ οὐκ ἔνδον. εὖ δέ σ᾽ ἐκφέρει
8κυνὸς Λακαίνης ὥς τις εὔρινος βάσις.
9ἔνδον γὰρ ἁνὴρ ἄρτι τυγχάνει, κάρα
10στάζων ἱδρῶτι καὶ χέρας ξιφοκτόνους.
11καί σ᾽ οὐδὲν εἴσω τῆσδε παπταίνειν πύλης
12ἔτ᾽ ἔργον ἐστίν, ἐννέπειν δ᾽ ὅτου χάριν
13σπουδὴν ἔθου τήνδ᾽, ὡς παρ᾽ εἰδυίας μάθῃς.
Ὀδ
14ὦ φθέγμ᾽ Ἀθάνας, φιλτάτης ἐμοὶ θεῶν,
15ὡς εὐμαθές σου, κἂν ἄποπτος ᾖς ὅμως,

Commentary

1ὦ παῖ Λαρτίου: Son of Laertes; i.e. Odysseus
1σε...ἁρπάσαι θηρώμενον: you hunting to snatch up; indirect discourse: present middle participle + aorist infinitive
1δέδορκά: 1st singular perfect of δέρκομαι
2πεῖράν τιν(α): some means of attack; “attempt”
2ἐχθρῶν: on..., against...; objective genitive
3καὶ: even; adverb with νῦν; responding to ἀεὶ μέν
3ἐπὶ σκηναῖς ναυτικαῖς...Αἴαντος: at...; the Greeks built their tents beside their ships
3σε...κυνηγετοῦντα καὶ μετρούμενον: you...; indirect discourse with present participles; present middle participle μετρέω means “measuring up (with the eyes)”
3ὁρῶ: 1st singular present of ὁράω
4τάξιν ἐσχάτην: farthest position (in the camp)
6ἴχνη: ἴχνεα, neuter plural accusative with νεοχάραχτ(α)
6τὰ (ἐ)κείνου: of that one; attributive position
6ὅπως ἴδῃς: so that you may...; purpose clause with 2nd singular aorist subjunctive of ὁράω
7εἴτ(ε)…εἴτ(ε)…: whether...or...
8κυνὸς...ὥς τις (βάσις) εὔρινος: just as the certain steps of...; clause of comparison
8βάσις: (your) steps; subject of ἐκφέρει
9κάρα…χέρας: on...and on...; accusative of respect
9τυγχάνει (ὤν): happens (to be)
11οὐδὲν...ἔργον ἐστίν: there is not any need to...
12ὅτου χάριν: for the sake of what...?; χάριν is here a preposition with genitive ὅστις (οὗτινος)
13ἔθου: made; ἔθε(σ)ο, 2nd singular aorist middle of τίθημι
13ὡς...μάθῃς: purpose, 2nd singular aorist subjunctive of μανθάνω
13παρ᾽ εἰδυίας: from her knowing; participle of οἶδα
15ὡς εὐμαθές...φώνημ᾽: how well known that voice
15κ(αὶ ἐ)ὰν…ᾖς: even if you are...; 2nd singular subjunctive of εἰμί

Ὀδ
16φώνημ᾽ ἀκούω καὶ ξυναρπάζω φρενὶ
17χαλκοστόμου κώδωνος ὡς Τυρσηνικῆς.
18καὶ νῦν ἐπέγνως εὖ μ᾽ ἐπ᾽ ἀνδρὶ δυσμενεῖ
19βάσιν κυκλοῦντ᾽, Αἴαντι τῷ σακεσφόρῳ·
20κεῖνον γάρ, οὐδέν᾽ ἄλλον, ἰχνεύω πάλαι.
21νυκτὸς γὰρ ἡμᾶς τῆσδε πρᾶγος ἄσκοπον
22ἔχει περάνας, εἴπερ εἴργασται τάδε·
23ἴσμεν γὰρ οὐδὲν τρανές, ἀλλ᾽ ἀλώμεθα·
24κἀγὼ 'θελοντὴς τῷδ᾽ ὑπεζύγην πόνῳ.
25ἐφθαρμένας γὰρ ἀρτίως εὑρίσκομεν
26λείας ἁπάσας καὶ κατηναρισμένας
27ἐκ χειρὸς αὐτοῖς ποιμνίων ἐπιστάταις.
28τήνδ᾽ οὖν ἐκείνῳ πᾶς τις αἰτίαν νέμει.
29καί μοί τις ὀπτὴρ αὐτὸν εἰσιδὼν μόνον
30πηδῶντα πεδία σὺν νεορράντῳ ξίφει

Commentary

15ὡς εὐμαθές...φώνημ᾽: how well known that voice
16ξυναρπάζω: turn old Attic ξυν- to συν-
16φρενὶ: in...; dative place where or means
17κώδωνος ὡς: just as from...; clause of comparison and genitive of source
18καὶ νῦν: and now
18μ(ε)...κυκλοῦντ(α): me...; indirect discourse, present participle
18ἐπέγνως: 2nd singular aorist
18ἐπ᾽ ἀνδρὶ δυσμενεῖ: upon...; dative δυσ-μενής
19Αἴαντι...σακεσφόρῳ: in apposition to ἀνδρὶ
20ἰχνεύω: I have been tracking; present, but πάλαι suggests a perfect-progressive sense
21νυκτὸς...τῆσδε: during...; genitive of time within which
21πρᾶγος ἄσκοπον: i.e. the slaughter of sheep
22ἔχει περάνας: has accomplished (acc.) for (acc.); periphrastic perfect (ἔχω + nominative aorist participle περαίνω) governing a double accusative
22εἴπερ εἴργασται τάδε: if actually he...; 3rd singular perfect middle of ἐργάζομαι; i.e. slaughter the sheep
23ἴσμεν: 1st plural of οἶδα
23οὐδέν(α) ἄλλον: in apposition to (ἐ)κεῖνον
23ἀλώμεθα: ἀλάομεθα; i.e. are adrift in doubt
24κ(αὶ ἐ)γὼ: and I...
24(ἐ)θελοντὴς: as a volunteer; i.e. voluntarily
24ὑπεζύγην: 1st singular aorist passive deponent + dative compound
25ἐφθαρμένας: perfect passive of φθείρω
26κατηναρισμένας: perfect passive of κατ-εναρίζω
27ἐκ χειρὸς: i.e. by a human being; genitive χείρ
27αὐτοῖς ἐπιστάταις: with overseers themselves
28ἐκείνῳ: on that one; i.e. Ajax, dative of interest
28πᾶς τις: every one
29εἰσιδὼν: nominative singular aorist participle of εἰσ-οράω
30πηδῶντα πεδία: bounding over the plain

Ὀδ
31φράζει τε κἀδήλωσεν· εὐθέως δ᾽ ἐγὼ
32κατ᾽ ἴχνος ᾁσσω, καὶ τὰ μὲν σημαίνομαι,
33τὰ δ᾽ ἐκπέπληγμαι κοὐκ ἔχω μαθεῖν ὅτου.
34καιρὸν δ᾽ ἐφήκεις· πάντα γὰρ τά τ᾽ οὖν πάρος
35τά τ᾽ εἰσέπειτα σῇ κυβερνῶμαι χερί.
Ἀθ
36ἔγνων, Ὀδυσσεῦ, καὶ πάλαι φύλαξ ἔβην
37τῇ σῇ πρόθυμος εἰς ὁδὸν κυναγίᾳ.
Ὀδ
38ἦ καί, φίλη δέσποινα, πρὸς καιρὸν πονῶ;
Ἀθ
39ὡς ἔστιν ἀνδρὸς τοῦδε τἄργα ταῦτά σοι.
Ὀδ
40καὶ πρὸς τί δυσλόγιστον ὧδ᾽ ᾖξεν χέρα;
Ἀθ
41χόλῳ βαρυνθεὶς τῶν Ἀχιλλείων ὅπλων.
Ὀδ
42τί δῆτα ποίμναις τήνδ᾽ ἐπεμπίπτει βάσιν;
Ἀθ
43δοκῶν ἐν ὑμῖν χεῖρα χραίνεσθαι φόνῳ.
Ὀδ
44ἦ καὶ τὸ βούλευμ᾽ ὡς ἐπ᾽ Ἀργείοις τόδ᾽ ἦν;
Ἀθ
45κἂν ἐξεπράξατ᾽, εἰ κατημέλησ᾽ ἐγώ.

Commentary

31φράζει τε κ(αὶ ἐ)δήλωσεν: both...and...
31εὐθέως: straightaway, immediately; adverb
32κατ(ὰ) ἴχνος: along..., on...
32τὰ (ἴχνη) μὲν...τὰ δ(ὲ): some (tracks)...as for others...; accusative object, and accusative of respect
32σημαίνομαι: I take as a sign; present middle
33ἐκπέπληγμαι: 1st singular perfect passive of ἐκ-πλήσσω
33κ(αὶ) οὐκ ἔχω: and I am not able...; “have the ability,” a common idiom for ἔχω + infinitive
33ὅτου: from...; genitive source from ὅστις (οὗτινος)
34καιρὸν ἐφήκεις: you arrived at the right time
34πάντα: in respect to...; accusative of respect
35τά τ(ε) πάρος… τά τ(ε) εἰσέπειτα: both those before and those hereafter; i.e. past and future
35σῇ...χερί: i.e. power; dative of means, χείρ
36ἔγνων: 1st singular aorist of γιγνώσκω
36φύλαξ: as a...; predicate nominative
36ἔβην: 1st singular aorist of βαίνω
37τῇ σῇ…κυναγίᾳ: for...; dative of compound adjective
37εἰς ὁδὸν: on...; governed by ἔβην
38ἦ καί: Am I actually...?; ἦ begins a question, and καί is intensive expressing surprise
38πρὸς καιρὸν: to the right point
39(ἴσθι) ὡς…τ(ὰ ἔ)ργα ταῦτά: (know) that these...; indirect discourse, add imperative οἶδα
39σοι: you know, you see; ethical dative
40πρὸς τί: to what purpose...?
40ᾖξεν: 3rd singular aorist of ἀίσσω
41βαρυνθεὶς: nominative singular aorist passive participle of βαρύνω
41τῶν...ὅπλων: at...; objective genitive with χόλῳ
42τί δῆτα: Why then...?; δῆτα is resumptive
43χεῖρα χραίνεσθαι: that he stains his hand
44ἦ καί: Is...actually...?; see the note on line 38
44ὡς ἐπ᾽ Ἀργείοις: as if against...
45κ(αὶ ἂ)ν: and he would have, if I had...; contrary-to-fact condition (εἰ aorist, ἄν + aorist)

Ὀδ
46ποίαισι τόλμαις ταῖσδε καὶ φρενῶν θράσει;
Ἀθ
47νύκτωρ ἐφ᾽ ὑμᾶς δόλιος ὁρμᾶται μόνος.
Ὀδ
48ἦ καὶ παρέστη κἀπὶ τέρμ᾽ ἀφίκετο;
Ἀθ
49καὶ δὴ 'πὶ δισσαῖς ἦν στρατηγίσιν πύλαις.
Ὀδ
50καὶ πῶς ἐπέσχε χεῖρα μαιμῶσαν φόνου;
Ἀθ
51ἐγώ σφ᾽ ἀπείργω, δυσφόρους ἐπ᾽ ὄμμασι
52γνώμας βαλοῦσα τῆς ἀνηκέστου χαρᾶς,
53καὶ πρός τε ποίμνας ἐκτρέπω σύμμικτά τε
54λείας ἄδαστα βουκόλων φρουρήματα·
55ἔνθ᾽ εἰσπεσὼν ἔκειρε πολύκερων φόνον
56κύκλῳ ῥαχίζων· κἀδόκει μὲν ἔσθ᾽ ὅτε
57δισσοὺς Ἀτρείδας αὐτόχειρ κτείνειν ἔχων,
58ὅτ᾽ ἄλλοτ᾽ ἄλλον ἐμπίτνων στρατηλατῶν.
59ἐγὼ δὲ φοιτῶντ᾽ ἄνδρα μανιάσιν νόσοις
60ὤτρυνον, εἰσέβαλλον εἰς ἕρκη κακά.

Commentary

46ποίαισι...τόλμαις...θράσει: by what sort of... and by what sort of...; dative of cause; θράσε-ι
46φρενῶν: of mind; partitive genitive of φρήν
47ἐφ᾽ ὑμᾶς: upon...; i.e. against
47δόλιος: deceitfully; translate the predicate adjective as an adverb
48ἦ καί παρέστη: Did he actually stand near? καί is intensive and expresses surprise
48κ(αὶ ἐ)πὶ τέρμ(α): and to the goal
49καὶ δὴ: already; δή is temporal, καί intensive
49(ἑ)πὶ δισσαῖς...στρατηγίσιν πύλαις: at...
49ἦν: 3rd singular imperfect of εἰμί
50φόνου: from...; genitive of separation with ἐπέσχε
51σφ(ε): him; accusative singular, σφεῖς
51δυσφόρους: i.e. irresistible, hard to resist
51ἐπ(ὶ) ὄμμασι: upon his eyes; dative plural of ὄμμα
52βαλοῦσα: by...; causal aorist participle of βάλλω
52τῆς...χαρᾶς: appositional genitive with γνώμας, or possibly genitive of separation with ἀπείργω
55εἰσπεσὼν: nominative singular aorist participle of εἰσ-πίπτω
55ἔκειρε: kept cutting down; iterative imperfect of κείρω
56κ(αὶ ἐ)δόκει: and he thought, and he imagined
56ἄλλοτ(ε) ἄλλον: different generals at different times; “one at one time, another at another time”
56ἔστ(ι) ὅτε... (ἐστὶ) ὅτε: one time...another time; an elliptical expression: “there is (a time) when”
60εἰς ἕρκη κακά: into troubled nets; ἕρκε-α

Ἀθ
61κἄπειτ᾽ ἐπειδὴ τοῦδ᾽ ἐλώφησεν πόνου,
62τοὺς ζῶντας αὖ δεσμοῖσι συνδήσας βοῶν
63ποίμνας τε πάσας εἰς δόμους κομίζεται,
64ὡς ἄνδρας, οὐχ ὡς εὔκερων ἄγραν ἔχων,
65καὶ νῦν κατ᾽ οἴκους συνδέτους αἰκίζεται.
66δείξω δὲ καὶ σοὶ τήνδε περιφανῆ νόσον,
67ὡς πᾶσιν Ἀργείοισιν εἰσιδὼν θροῇς.
68θαρσῶν δὲ μίμνε μηδὲ συμφορὰν δέχου
69τὸν ἄνδρ᾽· ἐγὼ γὰρ ὀμμάτων ἀποστρόφους
70αὐγὰς ἀπείρξω σὴν πρόσοψιν εἰσιδεῖν.
71οὗτος, σὲ τὸν τὰς αἰχμαλωτίδας χέρας
72δεσμοῖς ἀπευθύνοντα προσμολεῖν καλῶ·
73Αἴαντα φωνῶ· στεῖχε δωμάτων πάρος.
Ὀδ
74τί δρᾷς, Ἀθάνα; μηδαμῶς σφ᾽ ἔξω κάλει.
Ἀθ
75οὐ σῖγ᾽ ἀνέξει μηδὲ δειλίαν ἀρεῖ;

Commentary

61κ(αὶ ἔ)πειτ(α): and then
61τοῦδ᾽...πόνου: from...; genitive of separation
62τοὺς ζῶντας...βοῶν: the oxen still living; “the living of the oxen,” present participle of ζάω
62συνδήσας: nominative aorist participle of συν-δέω
63ποίμνας τε πάσας: and...; second accusative object
64ὡς ἄνδρας: as if...; clause of comparison
64οὐχ ὡς: not as if...; clause of comparison
65καὶ: even; adverb modifying νῦν
65κατ(ὰ) οἴκους: in the house
65συνδέτους: those bound; substantive
66δείξω: 1st singular future of δείκνυμι; σοι is dative indirect object
66καὶ: also, too; adverb
67ὡς...θροῇς: so that you may...; purpose with 2nd singular present subjunctive θροέω, “proclaim”; dative indirect object
67εἰσιδὼν: nominative singular aorist participle of εἰσ-οράω
68μίμνε...τὸν ἄνδρ(α): imperative and accusative object
68μηδὲ...δέχε(σ)ο: and do not accept it as a misfortune; middle imperative with double accusative
70αὐγὰς: the beams; i.e. his vision or sight
70ἀπείρξω: 1st singular future of ἀπείργω, “prevent”
70σὴν πρόσοψιν εἰσιδεῖν: from seeing...; aorist infinitive εἰσ-οράω governed by ἀπ-είργω
71οὗτος: You there!; i.e. Ajax; in exclamation
71τὸν...χέρας ἀπευθύνοντα: straightening their hands behind (ἀπό); i.e. binding; participle with σε
72προσμολεῖν: to come out; aorist infinitive of purpose
74σφ(ε): him; accusative singular, σφεῖς
74κάλει: καλε-ε, singular imperative; note the accent
75οὐ σῖγ(α) ἀνέξει μηδὲ δειλίαν ἀρεῖ: Will you not endure in silence and not earn a reputation of cowardice? 2nd singular future middle ἀνέξε(σ)αι, ἀρέ(σ)αι

ἀπευθύνω

76μὴ πρὸς θεῶν, ἀλλ᾽ ἔνδον ἀρκείτω μένων.
Ἀθ
77τί μὴ γένηται; πρόσθεν οὐκ ἀνὴρ ὅδ᾽ ἦν;
Ὀδ
78ἐχθρός γε τῷδε τἀνδρὶ καὶ τανῦν ἔτι.
Ἀθ
79οὔκουν γέλως ἥδιστος εἰς ἐχθροὺς γελᾶν;
Ὀδ
80ἐμοὶ μὲν ἀρκεῖ τοῦτον ἐν δόμοις μένειν.
Ἀθ
81μεμηνότ᾽ ἄνδρα περιφανῶς ὀκνεῖς ἰδεῖν;
Ὀδ
82φρονοῦντα γάρ νιν οὐκ ἂν ἐξέστην ὄκνῳ.
Ἀθ
83ἀλλ᾽ οὐδὲ νῦν σε μὴ παρόντ᾽ ἴδῃ πέλας.
Ὀδ
84πῶς, εἴπερ ὀφθαλμοῖς γε τοῖς αὐτοῖς ὁρᾷ;
Ἀθ
85ἐγὼ σκοτώσω βλέφαρα καὶ δεδορκότα.
Ὀδ
86γένοιτο μέντἂν πᾶν θεοῦ τεχνωμένου.
Ἀθ
87σίγα νυν ἑστὼς καὶ μέν᾽ ὡς κυρεῖς ἔχων.
Ὀδ
88μένοιμ᾽ ἄν· ἤθελον δ᾽ ἂν ἐκτὸς ὢν τυχεῖν.
Ἀθ
89ὦ οὕτος, Αἴας, δεύτερόν σε προσκαλῶ.
90τί βαιὸν οὕτως ἐντρέπει τῆς συμμάχου;

Commentary

76μὴ (κάλει), πρὸς θεῶν: Do not, by the gods
76ἔνδον...μένων: by...; causal nominative present participle
76ἀρκείτω: let him suffice; 3rd singular imperative of ἀρκέω
77τί μὴ γένηται: lest what happens?; fearing clause (μὴ + aorist subjunctive γίγνομαι)
77οὐκ ἦν;: Was he not...?; 3rd singular imperfect of εἰμί
78ἐχθρός γε: yes, an enemy...; γε is emphatic
78τῷδε τἀνδρὶ: to...; i.e. to Odysseus
79οὔκουν (ἐστίν): (Is) not then...; γέλως ἥδιστος is predicate, and infinitive γελᾶν is the subject
80σίγα...μέν(ε): be silent...and remain; imperatives
80ἀρκεῖ: it suffices; impersonal + dative of reference
80τοῦτον...μένειν: that this one...; accusative subject + infinitive
81μεμηνότα: accusative perfect participle of μαίνομαι; the perfect denotes a state rather than an activity: ‘being mad’
81ἰδεῖν: from seeing; aorist infinitive of ὁράω
82φρονοῦντα: (if)...; participle conditional in sense
82οὐκ ἂν ἐξέστην: I would not stand out of the way of (accusative); contrary to fact (ἂν + 1st singular aorist indicative)
82ὄκνῳ: by...; dative of means
83οὐδὲ νῦν μὴ...ἴδῃ: not even now (perhaps) would he...; οὐ μή + aorist subjunctive in a doubtful negation (Smyth 1801)
83παρόντ(α) πέλας: (although)...; present participle
84ὀφθαλμοῖς γε τοῖς αὐτοῖς: with...; αὐτός in attributive position means ‘same’
85σκοτώσω: 1st singular future
85καὶ δεδορκότα: even though...; perfect participle of δέρκομαι, concessive in sense; καί is adverbial
86γένοιτο μέντ(οι) ἂν πᾶν: certainly, anything could happen; potential aorist optative of γίγνομαι
86θεοῦ τεχνωμένου: genitive absolute
87σίγα...μέν(ε): be silent...and remain; imperatives
87ἑστὼς: nominative singular perfect participle of ἵστημι
87ὡς κυρεῖς ἔχων: as you happen to be disposed; κυρέω + participle; ἔχω + adverb means ‘be disposed’
88ἤθελον δ᾽ ἂν: I would wish; contrary to fact
88ὢν τυχεῖν: to happen to be; τυγχάνω + participle
89οὗτος: You there!; i.e. Ajax, in exclamation
90τί βαιὸν οὕτως ἐντρέπε(σ)αι: why do you show so slight regard to; βαιόν is an inner accusative

94καλῶς ἔλεξας· ἀλλ᾽ ἐκεῖνό μοι φράσον,

97ἦ καὶ πρὸς Ἀτρείδαισιν ᾔχμασας χέρα;

98ὥστ᾽ οὔποτ᾽ Αἴανθ᾽ οἵδ᾽ ἀτιμάσουσ᾽ ἔτι.
Ἀθ
99τεθνᾶσιν ἄνδρες, ὡς τὸ σὸν ξυνῆκ᾽ ἐγώ.
Αἴ
100θανόντες ἤδη τἄμ᾽ ἀφαιρείσθων ὅπλα.
Ἀθ
101εἶεν, τί γὰρ δὴ παῖς ὁ τοῦ Λαερτίου,
102ποῦ σοι τύχης ἕστηκεν; ἢ πέφευγέ σε;
Αἴ
103ἦ τοὐπίτριπτον κίναδος ἐξήρου μ᾽ ὅπου;

104ἔγωγ᾽· Ὀδυσσέα τὸν σὸν ἐνστάτην λέγω.

Commentary

91ὦ...Ἀθάνα: vocative, direct address
91χαῖρ(ε): hello! Welcome!; singular imperative
91Διογενὲς τέκνον: vocative, direct address
92ὡς εὖ παρέστης: How well you have stood by me!; in exclamation; 2nd singular pluperfect indicative of παρ-ίστημι; i.e. ‘you had stood by and continue to do so’
93στέψω: future
93χάριν: in return for + preceding genitive
94καλῶς: well; adverb
94ἔλεξας: 2nd singular aorist of λέγω, equivalent to εἶπες
94φράσον: aorist imperative of φράζω and dative indirect object
95ἔβαψας: 2nd singular aorist of βάπτω; i.e. in red blood
95πρὸς Ἀργείων στρατῷ: near..., before...
96πάρεστι: is there; i.e. Yes, I can boast
96κ(αὶ) οὐκ ἀπαρνοῦμαι τὸ μή (δρᾶσαι): and I do not deny doing it; after verbs of prohibiting an infinitive (here, articular infinitive) takes a redundant μή to confirm the negative of the main verb (Smyth 2739)
97ἦ καὶ: Did you actually...?; καί is intensive
97πρὸς...: against...
97ᾔχμασας: 2nd singular aorist of αἰχμάζω with accusative singular χείρ
98Αἴαντ(α): accusative singular of Αἴας
99τεθνᾶσιν: are dead; 3rd plural perfect of θνῄσκω
99ἔγωγ(ε): Yes, I did
99ὡς...ξυνῆκ(α): as I understand...; clause of comparison; 1st singular aorist of συν-ίημι, ‘put together’
99τὸ σὸν: your remarks
100θανόντες: the dead; subject, aorist of θνῄσκω
100τἄμ᾽: my; τὰ ἐμά modifying ὅπλα
100ἀφαιρείσθων: let them take away; 3rd plural imperative
101οἵδ(ε) ἀτιμάσουσ(ι): these men...; 3rd plural future
101τί γὰρ δὴ: Just what then about...?; no verb
102ποῦ...τύχης: where of bad fortune...
102ἕστηκεν: does he stand; perfect of ἵστημι
103ὅπου τ(ὸ) ἐπίτριπτον κίναδος (ἐστί): where the accursed fox is...
103ἐξήρε(σ)ο μ(ε): 2nd singular aorist middle of ἐξ-έρομαι
104λέγω: I mean
105ἥδιστος: most pleasing; i.e. for Ajax

Commentary

106θανεῖν: aorist infinitive of θνῄσκω
106οὔ τί: not at all; indefinite τι is adverbial accusative
107πρὶν ἂν τί δράσῃς: Until you do what?; πρὶν clause, anticipatory subjunctive ἄν + aorist subjunctive δράω
107ἢ τί κερδάνῃς πλέον: or what more...?; a second question with anticipatory aorist subjunctive; add πρὶν ἄν
108πρὶν ἂν: until; repeated without verb in reply
108(πρὶν ἂν) θάνῃ: before he dies; 3rd singular aorist subjunctive
108δεθεὶς: nominative singular aorist passive participle of δέω
108ἑρκείου στέγης: of my home dwelling; via synecdoche, ‘roof’ can mean ‘dwelling’
109τί δῆτα...κακόν: What harm then...?
109ἐργάσει: ἐργάσεσαι, 2nd singular future middle of ἐργάζομαι
110νῶτα: on...; accusative of respect
110φοινιχθεὶς: made red; nominative aorist passive participle
111μὴ δῆτα...αἰκίσῃ: Now don’t...; prohibitive subjunctive (μὴ + aorist subjunctive); 2nd singular aorist subjunctive of αἰκίζομαι
111ὧδέ γ(ε): in this way at least; γε is restrictive
112τ(ὰ) ἂλλ(α): in other respects; accusative of respect
112ἐφίεμαι: I bid you rejoice...; 1st singular present middle of ἐφίημι
113τίσει: future of τίνω
113κ(αὶ) οὐκ ἄλλην: and no other; after τήνδε
114τοιάνδε...σύμμαχον παρεστάναι: namely that you stand by as such an ally to me; accusative predicate
114οὖν: then, accordingly; inferential
114ἐπειδὴ...ἥδε (ἐστίν): Since this is...
114τὸ δρᾶν: to do; just as an explanatory infinitive, this articular infinitive is accusative of respect with τέρψις
115χρα(σ)ο: use + dative; middle imperative of χράομαι
115φείδε(σ)ο: middle imperative of φείδομαι
116σοὶ τοῦτ(ο) ἐφίεμαι: I bid this to you
118τὴν...ἰσχὺν ὅση: how great the strength is; proleptic accusative: make ἰσχύν predicate in the question
119τούτου...τἀνδρὸς: than...; genitive of comparison
119τίς ἄν...ηὑρέθη: Who could have been found to be; contrary to fact (ἄν, aorist passive εὑρίσκω)
119ἢ...ἢ: either...or...
120δρᾶν: to do; explanatory infinitive after ἀμείνων

Commentary

122καίπερ ὄντα δυσμενῆ: although...; present participle of εἰμί concessive in sense; δυσμενέα is accusative predicate
123ἄτῃ...κακῇ: with..., to...; dative of compound verb
123συγκατέζευκται: perfect passive; translate ‘is Xed’
124οὐδὲν...μᾶλλον ἢ: not at all more than, no more than; οὐδέν is adverbial accusative (accusative of extent of degree: ‘more by nothing’)
124οὐδέν(α) οἶδ(α): in reply
124τὸ (ἐ)μὸν: my own lot
124τὸ τούτου: this one’s lot; ‘that of this one’
125οὐδὲν ἄλλο πλὴν: nothing other except...
125ὄντας: present participle of εἰμί
126ὅσοιπερ ζῶμεν: as many as live; relative clause with 1st plural present ζάω; ἡμᾶς is the antecedent
126ἢ: or; joining εἴδωλα and κούφην σκιάν
127τοιαῦτα...εἰσορῶν: while seeing such things; present participle
128μηδέν ποτ᾽ εἴπῃς: Do not ever...; prohibitive subjunctive (μὴ + aorist subjunctive); 2nd singular λέγω; translate ‘one’ or ‘any’ in μηδέν with ὑπέρκοπον ἔπος
128αὐτὸς: yourself; intensive pronoun
128εἰς θεοὺς: toward..., against...
129μηδ(ὲ)...ἄρῃ: nor lift up...; prohibitive subjunctive (μὴ + aorist subjunctive); 2nd singular aorist middle of αἴρω
129ὄγκον μηδέν(α): any puffed-up pride, gravitas
129εἴ...πλέον βρίθεις: if you are more mighty...
129τινος: than...; genitive of comparison
130ἢ χειρὶ...ἢ...βάθει: either in...or in...; dative of respect; by metonymy, χείρ means ‘power’
131ὡς: inasmuch as, or for/since; introduces a causal clause
131κ(αὶ) ἀνάγει: and brings back; 3rd singular of ἀν-άγω
135ἔχων βάθρον: holding the solid foundation

136σὲ μὲν εὖ πράσσοντ᾽ ἐπιχαίρω·
137σὲ δ᾽ ὅταν πληγὴ Διὸς ἢ ζαμενὴς
138λόγος ἐκ Δαναῶν κακόθρους ἐπιβῇ,
139μέγαν ὄκνον ἔχω καὶ πεφόβημαι
140πτηνῆς ὡς ὄμμα πελείας.
141ὡς καὶ τῆς νῦν φθιμένης νυκτὸς
142μεγάλοι θόρυβοι κατέχουσ᾽ ἡμᾶς
143ἐπὶ δυσκλείᾳ, σὲ τὸν ἱππομανῆ
144λειμῶν᾽ ἐπιβάντ᾽ ὀλέσαι Δαναῶν
145βοτὰ καὶ λείαν,
146ἥπερ δορίληπτος ἔτ᾽ ἦν λοιπή,
147κτείνοντ᾽ αἴθωνι σιδήρῳ.
148τοιούσδε λόγους ψιθύρους πλάσσων
149εἰς ὦτα φέρει πᾶσιν Ὀδυσσεύς,
150καὶ σφόδρα πείθει· περὶ γὰρ σοῦ νῦν

Commentary

136εὖ πράσσοντ(α): when faring well; idiom
137ἢ ζαμενὴς λόγος: or raging rumor
137ὅταν...ἐπιβῇ: whenever...; general temporal clause with ἄν + 3rd singular aorist subjunctive ἐπι-βαίνω
139πεφόβημαι: perfect middle of φοβέω denotes a state, not an activity; ‘am Xed’ rather than ‘Xed’
140ὡς ὄμμα: just as...; clause of comparison; i.e. quick moving and skittish
141ὡς καὶ: so too, so also; in contrast to ὅταν...
141τῆς νῦν φθιμένης νυκτὸς: during...; genitive of time within
142μεγάλοι θόρυβοι: loud uproars, loud clamors; θόρυβος refers to the noise of a crowd
142κατέχουσι: take hold of; or possibly ‘spread’ or ‘fill’ (i.e. ‘hold over’)
143ἐπὶ δυσκλείᾳ: to the point of disgrace
143ἐπιβάντ(α): accusative singular aorist participle of ἐπι-βαίνω modifying accusative subject σέ
143σὲ...ὀλέσαι: namely that you...; indirect discourse with aorist infinitive ὄλλυμι in apposition to θόρυβοι
143τὸν ἱππομανέ-α λειμῶν(α): accusative singular object
145βοτὰ καὶ λείαν: the beasts of plunder; literally ‘beasts and plunder’; hendiadys, two terms describing a single object
146ἥπερ...ἦν: which...; 3rd singular imperfect of εἰμί
146λοιπή: left over after the distribution
147κτείνοντ(α): participle; assume βοτὰ καὶ λείαν as object
147αἴθωνι σιδήρῳ: with...; dative of means; i.e. swords and spearpoint
149ὦτα: neuter accusative plural of οὖς
149πᾶσιν: of all, for all; dative of possession from πᾶς
150σφόδρα: exceedingly well
150περὶ...σοῦ: concerning you

151εὔπειστα λέγει, καὶ πᾶς ὁ κλύων
152τοῦ λέξαντος χαίρει μᾶλλον
153τοῖς σοῖς ἄχεσιν καθυβρίζων.
154τῶν γὰρ μεγάλων ψυχῶν ἱεὶς
155οὐκ ἂν ἁμάρτοις· κατὰ δ᾽ ἄν τις ἐμοῦ
156τοιαῦτα λέγων οὐκ ἂν πείθοι·
157πρὸς γὰρ τὸν ἔχονθ᾽ ὁ φθόνος ἕρπει.
158καίτοι σμικροὶ μεγάλων χωρὶς
159σφαλερὸν πύργου ῥῦμα πέλονται·
160μετὰ γὰρ μεγάλων βαιὸς ἄριστ᾽ ἂν
161καὶ μέγας ὀρθοῖθ᾽ ὑπὸ μικροτέρων.
162ἀλλ᾽ οὐ δυνατὸν τοὺς ἀνοήτους
163τούτων γνώμας προδιδάσκειν.
164ὑπὸ τοιούτων ἀνδρῶν θορυβεῖ
165χἠμεῖς οὐδὲν σθένομεν πρὸς ταῦτ᾽

Commentary

151εὔπειστα: things easily persuasive
151πᾶς ὁ κλύων: each one, when listening; participle
152τοῦ λέξαντος: than the one saying it; genitive of comparison following μᾶλλον; aorist participle of λέγω
152χαίρει...καθυβρίζων: rejoices in insulting; χαίρω with present participle
153τοῖς σοῖς ἄχεσιν: dative of compound verb; ἄχος; translate as the object of καθυβρίζων
154τῶν...μεγάλων ψυχῶν: at...; partitive genitive often follows verbs of aiming
154ἱείς: aiming at, launching, sending; nominative singular present participle of ἵημι
155οὐκ ἂν ἁμάρτοις: you would not miss; potential optative, ἄν + 2nd singular aorist optative of ἁμαρτάνω
155κατὰ δ᾽ ἐμοῦ: but against me
156λέγων: if saying; present participle conditional in sense
156οὐκ ἂν πείθοι: he would not persuade; potential optative, ἄν + 3rd singular present optative of πείθω
157πρὸς τὸν ἔχοντα: toward the one having much, i.e. the powerful or rich; present participle of ἔχω
158σμικροί: small men; substantive and subject
158μεγάλων: great men; genitive object of χωρίς
159πύργου ῥῦμα: protection for city walls; πύργου is objective genitive or appositional genitive
160μετὰ γὰρ...ὑπὸ μικροτέρων: for the small man is best set upright with the great, and the great by the smaller men
160ἄριστα: superlative adverb
160ἂν ὀρθοῖτο: 3rd singular potential optative, present of ὀρθόω
162δυνατὸν ἐστίν: it is possible; impersonal expression
162τοὺς ἀνοήτους: that the foolish; accusative subject
163τούτων γνώμας: judgments in these matters; objective genitive
164ὑπὸ τοιούτων ἀνδρῶν: by such men, i.e. the foolish
164θορυβεῖ: there is an uproar; impersonal
165χἠμεῖς: and we; κ(αὶ) ἡμεῖς
165οὐδέν: not at all; adverbial accusative (inner accusative)
165πρὸς ταῦτα: against these things

166ἀπαλέξασθαι σοῦ χωρίς, ἄναξ.
167ἀλλ᾽ ὅτε γὰρ δὴ τὸ σὸν ὄμμ᾽ ἀπέδραν,
168παταγοῦσιν ἅπερ πτηνῶν ἀγέλαι·
169μέγαν αἰγυπιὸν δ᾽ ὑποδείσαντες
170τάχ᾽ ἂν ἐξαίφνης, εἰ σὺ φανείης,
171σιγῇ πτήξειαν ἄφωνοι.
172ἦ ῥά σε Ταυροπόλα Διὸς Ἄρτεμις—
173ὦ μεγάλα φάτις, ὦ
174μᾶτερ αἰσχύνας ἐμᾶς—
175ὥρμασε πανδάμους ἐπὶ βοῦς ἀγελαίας,
176ἦ πού τινος νίκας ἀκάρπωτον χάριν,
177ἤ ῥα κλυτῶν ἐνάρων
178ψευσθεῖσ᾽, ἀδώροις, εἴτ᾽ ἐλαφαβολίας;
179ἢ χαλκοθώραξ μή τιν᾽ Ἐνυάλιος
180μομφὰν ἔχων ξυνοῦ δορὸς ἐννυχίοις

Commentary

166ἀπαλέξασθαι: to defend; aorist middle infinitive
166σοῦ χωρίς: they are powerless without you
166ἄναξ: vocative, direct address; i.e. Ajax
167ἀλλὰ γάρ: but in fact; γάρ is adverbial
167ὅτε...δή: exactly when; δή is intensive
167ἀπέδραν: 3rd plural aorist of ἀπο-διδράσκω
168ἅπερ πτηνῶν ἀγέλαι: just as flocks of birds; a relative clause of comparison
169δ᾽ ὑποδείσαντες: but having feared; aorist participle of ὑπο-δείδω
170εἰ...φανείης, ἂν...πτήξειαν: if you should appear, they would cower; future less vivid condition, εἰ + optative, ἄν + optative
172ἦ...σε Ταυροπόλα...Ἄρτεμις...ὥρμασε: Did Artemis set you in motion? nominative subject and 3rd singular aorist of ὁρμάω
172ῥά: it turns out, therefore; = ἄρα
172Διός: daughter of Zeus; genitive singular
173ὦ μεγάλα φάτις: O great rumor; vocative
173ὦ μᾶτερ αἰσχύνας ἐμᾶς: O mother of my shame, i.e. rumor
175πανδάμους ἐπὶ βοῦς ἀγελαίας: against public herds of cattle; literally cattle in herds
176ἦ πού...ἀκάρπωτον: was it, I suppose, a lack of offering of gratitude?
176τινος νίκας χάριν: for the sake of some victory
177ἤ ῥα...ψευσθεῖσα...εἴτε: either, as it seems, by being cheated...or; aorist passive participle
177κλυτῶν ἐνάρων: from famous spoils; genitive of separation
178ἀδώροις: by a lack of gifts; dative of cause
178ἐλαφαβολίας: from deer-hunting; genitive of separation
179ἤ...τινα μομφὰν ἔχων...δορός: or by having some cause for anger for a shared spearfight
180ἐννυχίοις μαχαναῖς: by machinations at night, i.e. compelling Ajax to slaughter cattle

181μαχαναῖς ἐτίσατο λώβαν;
183οὔ ποτε γὰρ φρενόθεν γ᾽ ἐπ᾽ ἀριστερά,
184παῖ Τελαμῶνος, ἔβας
185τόσσον, ἐν ποίμναις πίτνων·
186ἥκοι γὰρ ἂν θεία νόσος· ἀλλ᾽ ἀπερύκοι
187καὶ Ζεὺς κακὰν καὶ Φοῖβος Ἀργείων φάτιν.
188εἰ δ᾽ ὑποβαλλόμενοι
189κλέπτουσι μύθους οἱ μεγάλοι βασιλῆς
190ἢ τᾶς ἀσώτου Σισυφιδᾶν γενεᾶς,
191μὴ μή, ἄναξ, ἔθ᾽ ὧδ᾽ ἐφάλοις κλισίαις
192ὄμμ᾽ ἔχων κακὰν φάτιν ἄρῃ.
193ἀλλ᾽ ἄνα ἐξ ἑδράνων, ὅπου μακραίωνι
194στηρίζῃ ποτὲ τᾷδ᾽ ἀγωνίῳ σχολᾷ
195ἄταν οὐρανίαν φλέγων.

Commentary

180ἐννυχίοις μαχαναῖς: by machinations at night, i.e. compelling Ajax to slaughter cattle
183φρενόθεν γ᾽: from your own mind, at least; γε is restrictive and emphatic
183ἐπ᾽ ἀριστερά: upon a sinister path; literally to the left side, i.e. on a wrong course of action
184ἔβας: 2nd singular aorist of βαίνω
185τόσσον: so far; adverbial accusative of τόσος, an inner accusative
185πίτνων: by falling; nominative singular present participle causal in sense; poetic form for πίπτων
186ἥκοι...ἂν: could have come; potential optative of ἥκω
186ἀπερύκοι...κακὰν...φάτιν: may Zeus and Phoebus ward off the evil rumor; optative of wish
188ὑποβαλλόμενοι: present middle participle
189κλέπτουσι μύθους: tell stories by stealth
189βασιλῆς: kings; βασιλέες, i.e. sons of Atreus
190ἢ τᾶς ἀσώτου Σισυφιδᾶν γενεᾶς: or the one of the unsavable race of descendants of Sisyphus; i.e. Odysseus, a second nominative subject
191μὴ...ἐτίσατο λώβαν: surely did not pay back an outrage; aorist middle of τίνω; a question expecting “no”
191μὴ μή...ἄρῃ: Do not, do not raise up; prohibitive subjunctive, μὴ + aorist subjunctive of αἴρω
191ἐφάλοις κλισίαις: in the seaside huts; dative of place where
192ὄμμα ἔχων: by keeping your face hidden
193ἄνα: Up! Rise! from ἀνά with anastrophe
193μακραίωνι...σχολᾷ: in this long-lived rest from battle; dative of time when
193ὅπου στηρίζεσαι ποτέ: wherever you are settled; 2nd singular present middle
195ἄταν...φλέγων: making ruin blaze up

196ἀτάρβητα: fearlessly; predicate adjective used as an adverb

221οἵαν ἐδήλωσας ἀνέρος αἴθονος

214οὐκ...ἄϊδρις: not unknowingly, i.e. with knowledge; predicate adjective used as an adverb
215πῶς δῆτα λέγω: how then am I to speak? λέγω is a deliberative present subjunctive
215λόγον ἄρρητον: unspeakable words, i.e. shameful words
216ἐκπεύσεσαι: 2nd singular future of ἐκ-πυνθάνομαι
216βάρος: a heavy burden; object, i.e. suffering
217μανίᾳ: by madness; dative of means with ἁλούς
217ἁλούς: nominative singular aorist participle of ἁλίσκομαι
217ἡμίν: our; dative of possession
218ἀπελωβήθη: was dishonored, was disgraced; 3rd singular aorist passive; note the lack of agency
219τοιαῦτα: such things, i.e. the following
219ἂν ἴδοις: you could see; 2nd singular potential aorist optative of ὁράω
219bσφάγια αἱμοβαφέα: blood-stained victims; neuter accusative plural
221οἵαν...ἀγγελίαν: what sort of report! in exclamation
221ἐδήλωσας: 2nd singular aorist of δηλόω
221ἀνέρος αἴθονος: about a fiery man; objective genitive with ἀγγελίαν; ἀνέρος is genitive singular of ἀνήρ and alternative to ἀνδρός

225κλῃζομέναν: present passive participle

236bδύο δ᾽ ἀργίποδας κριοὺς ἀνελὼν
238τοῦ μὲν κεφαλὴν καὶ γλῶσσαν ἄκραν
239ῥίπτει θερίσας, τὸν δ᾽ ὀρθὸν ἄνω
240κίονι δήσας

Commentary

226τὰν ὁ μέγας μῦθος ἀέξει: which...; here as a relative pronoun; μῦθος refers to the rumor
227οἴμοι: Ah me!, Woe is me!; in exclamation
227τὸ προσέρπον: what is...; neuter accusative participle as a substantive, i.e. the rumor or report
228περίφαντος: translate a predicate adjective as an adverb
228θανεῖται: future middle θνῄσκω (future stem θανε-)
229παραπλάκτῳ χερὶ: with...; dative of means or manner, χείρ
229συγκατακτὰς: nominative singular aorist participle συγ-κατα-κτείνω
230κελαινοῖς ξίφεσιν: dative of means, ξίφος
231ὤμοι: Ah me!, Woe is me!; in exclamation
231κεῖθεν: from there, then; i.e. after Ajax slaughtered the animals
231ἡμῖν: to me, i.e. toward me; dative often follows verbs of motion; Tecmessa likely uses a royal we
234δεσμῶτιν ποίμνην: captive flock; attributive apposition
234ἤλυθε: 3rd singular aorist ἔρχομαι
235ὧν: among which...; partitive genitive referring to ποίμνην individually
235τὴν μὲν... τὰ δὲ: some...but others...; the flock considered individually
235σφάζ᾽: he would...; 3rd singular customary imperfect σφάζω
235ἐπὶ: upon...
236ἀνερρήγνυ: he would...; 3rd singular customary imperfect
236bἀνελὼν: nominative singular aorist participle ἀν-αιρέω
238τοῦ μὲν... τὸν δ᾽: of one...the other; i.e. rams
238γλῶσσαν ἄκραν: tip of the tongue
239ῥίπτει: threw away; 3rd singular imperfect ῥίπτω
239θερίσας: nominative singular aorist participle
239ὀρθὸν: upright; predicate adjective
240κίονι: on...; dative place where
240δήσας: nominative singular aorist participle δέω, bind

255τὸν...ἴσχει: whom...holds; relative clause

Commentary

256λαμπρᾶς γὰρ ἄτερ στεροπῆς...νότος ὣς: just as the south wind...; clause of comparison with verb omitted; ἄτερ + genitive
257ᾁξας ὀξὺς: after darting sharply; singular aorist participle ἀίσσω; translate predicate adjective as adverb
257λήγει: Ajax grows calm; main verb
258καὶ νῦν: and now
258φρόνιμος: Ajax is in his right mind
260τὸ ἐσλεύσσειν: looking on...; nominative subject
260οἰκεῖα πάθη: self-made sufferings, his own sufferings; neuter accusative plural
261μηδενὸς ἄλλου παραπράξαντος: no one else contributing; genitive absolute conditional in sense
262ὑποτείνει: extends, lays out, offers
263εἰ πέπαυται...δοκῶ: if he has stopped, I think...; simple present condition
263ἂν εὐτυχεῖν: that he/we/it may be well; indirect discourse, ἂν + infinitive equivalent to potential optative
264φρούδου γὰρ ἤδη τοῦ κακοῦ μείων λόγος: the accounting or concern of trouble already past is less
265πότερα δ᾽: Which...? introducing an alternative question
265ἄν, εἰ νέμοι..., λάβοις: would you choose, if one should give; future less vivid condition
266φίλους ἀνιῶν αὐτὸς ἡδονὰς ἔχειν: that you yourself have pleasures while causing grief to friends; indirect discourse
267ἢ κοινὸς ἐν κοινοῖσι λυπεῖσθαι ξυνών: or that you, being together, be grieved along in common; indirect discourse
268τό διπλάζον (ἐστίν): the two-fold pain is
270πῶς...ἔλεξας: What do you mean by this? idiom with aorist λέγω
270ὅπως λέγεις: what you mean; idiom

316ἔλεξα πᾶν ὅσονπερ ἐξηπιστάμην.
317ὁ δ᾽ εὐθὺς ἐξῴμωξεν οἰμωγὰς λυγράς,
318ἃς οὔποτ᾽ αὐτοῦ πρόσθεν εἰσήκουσ᾽ ἐγώ·
319πρὸς γὰρ κακοῦ τε καὶ βαρυψύχου γόους
320τοιούσδ᾽ ἀεί ποτ᾽ ἀνδρὸς ἐξηγεῖτ᾽ ἔχειν·
321ἀλλ᾽ ἀψόφητος ὀξέων κωκυμάτων
322ὑπεστέναζε ταῦρος ὣς βρυχώμενος.
323νῦν δ᾽ ἐν τοιᾷδε κείμενος κακῇ τύχῃ
324ἄσιτος ἁνήρ, ἄποτος, ἐν μέσοις βοτοῖς
325σιδηροκμῆσιν ἥσυχος θακεῖ πεσών·
326καὶ δῆλός ἐστιν ὥς τι δρασείων κακόν.
327τοιαῦτα γάρ πως καὶ λέγει κὠδύρεται.
328ἀλλ᾽, ὦ φίλοι, τούτων γὰρ οὕνεκ᾽ ἐστάλην,
329ἀρήξατ᾽ εἰσελθόντες, εἰ δύνασθέ τι·
330φίλων γὰρ οἱ τοιοίδε νικῶνται λόγοις.

Commentary

316ἔλεξα: 1s aor. λέγω
317ὁ δ(ὲ)...ἐξῴμωξεν: and he...; aor. ἐξ-οιμώζω
318ἃς...εἰσήκουσ(α): which...; relative clause
318αὐτοῦ: from...; gen. of source
319πρὸς κακοῦ τε καὶ βαρυψύχου...ἀνδρὸς: in (the nature/way of) a cowardly and heavy-hearted man; unusual πρός + gen. describing a general characteristic: make the pred. of ἔχειν
319γόους τοιούσδ᾽…ἔχειν: that such wailings are...; ind. disc.; ἔχειν ‘are disposed’ or ‘hold’
320ἐξηγεῖτ(ο): he used to explain, would explain; customary impf., 3s impf. mid. ἐξ-ηγέομαι
322ὑπεστέναζε: he used to...; customary impf.
322ταῦρος ὣς: just as...; clause of comparison
323νῦν δ(ὲ): but now…; in contrast
325πεσών: aor. pple πίπτω; i.e. where he fell
326δῆλός ἐστιν ὥς…δρασείων: he clearly has in mind to do...; δῆλός ἐστιν + pple; ὥς is here superfluous (cf. δῆλόν ἐστι ὡς = it is clear that)
327καὶ λέγει κ(αὶ) ὀδύρεται: he both...and...
328τούτων οὕνεκ(α): for the sake of this; οὕνεκα, ‘because of which’ is here a preposition ἕνεκα
328ἐστάλην: I set out; 1s aor. pass. στέλλω; lit. ‘I was sent out by myself’ or ‘I sent myself out’
329ἀρήξατ(ε): 2p aor. imperative ἀρήγω
329εἰ δύνασθέ τι: if you are at all able; inner acc.
330οἱ τοιοίδε: such men; i.e. as Ajax
330νικῶνται: pres. pass. νικάω, ‘win over’

Commentary

331δεινά: neut. acc. pl. substantive: add ‘things’
332ἡμῖν: dat. ind. obj.
332τὸν ἄνδρα διαπεφοιβάσθαι: (namely) that...; ind. disc. with pf. pass. inf. in apposition to δεινά; pf. tense denotes a state: ‘is Xed’
332κακοῖς: dat. of means
333ἰώ μοί μοι: Ah me, me!; an exclamation by Ajax, who is entering from offstage
334τάχ(α)…μᾶλλον: soon even more; in response to τὸν ἄνδρα διαπεφοιβάσθαι above
334ὡς ἔοικε: as it seems; parenthetical clause of comparison
335Αἴαντος: proleptic gen. of source (‘from Ajax’): translate as the subject of θωΰσσει
335οἵαν τήνδε θωΰσσει βοήν: what sort of cry...; ind. question
336ἰώ μοί μοι: Ah me, me!; an exclamation
337τοῖς..νοσήμασιν ξυνοῦσι: by...; dat. of means and dat. pl. pres. pple σύν-ειμι
337(ὁ) ἀνὴρ: the man
337ἢ...ἢ: either...or...; with complementary infs. governed by ἔοικεν
338παρών: being there; pple πάρ-ειμι
339ἰὼ παῖ παῖ: Ah my son, my son!
340ὤμοι τάλαιν(α): Woe is me, wretched!; fem. nom. sg. τάλας, τάλαινα
340Εὐρύσακες: voc. direct address; the name of Ajax’s son, which means ‘broad-shield’
340ἀμφὶ σοὶ: about you, concerning you
340βοᾷ: Ajax as subject; βοά-ει, 3s pres. βοάω
341τί ποτε: what in the world...?; ‘what ever,’ as often expressing surprise; 3s pres. μενοινάω
341ποῦ ποτ᾽: Where in the world...?; ‘where ever,’ expressing surprise, 2s pres. εἰμί; Tecmessa turns away from Eurysaces and talks to Ajax
341τάλαιν(α) ἐγώ: Wretched I (am)!
342τὸν εἰσαεὶ...χρόνον: for...; acc. of duration
342ποῦ (ἔστίν) Τεῦκρος; Teucer is Ajax’ brother
343ἐγὼ δ᾽ ἀπόλλυμαι: while I am perishing
344(ὁ ἀ)νὴρ: the man
344φρονεῖν: to be of right mind, to be in his senses
344ἀνοίγετε: i.e. the door; 2s pres. imperative

345βλέψας: (when)...; nom. aor. pple βλέπω

Commentary

346ἰδού: look! Behold!; ἰδέ(σ)ο a common 2s aor. mid. imperative ὁράω
346διοίγω: I am opening (the doors); δι-οίγνυμι
346ἔξεστί: it is possible, it is allowed; impersonal
346σοι: for...; dat. of interest
347τὰ...πράγε-α: neut. pl., πρᾶγος
347τοῦδε: i.e. of Ajax
347κα(ὶ) αὐτὸς ὡς ἔχων κυρεῖ: and how he himself happens to be; ind. question with interrogative adv. ὡς, ‘how;’ 3s κυρέω governs a complementary pple; ἔχω, ‘is disposed,’ + adv. is often equiv. to εἰμί + pred.; αὐτὸς should be acc. but is attracted into the nom. of the ind. question
348ἰὼ: Ah!
349φίλοι ναυβάται: voc. dir. address
350ὀρθῷ νόμῳ: by righteous custom, by the correct rule; i.e. of friendship; dat. compound
351ἴδεσθέ: 2p aor. mid. imperative ὁράω
351οἷον...κῦμα...κυκλεῖται: what sort of wave...; ind. question, μέ is obj. of pres. mid. κυκλέω
351φοινίας ὑπὸ ζάλης: (caused) by...; lit. ‘because of...’ or ‘by,’ ὑπό + gen. expressing cause; this storm causes the wave (κῦμα) of blood
354οἴμ(οι): Ah me! Woe is me!
354ὡς...ὀρθὰ...ἄγαν: How too correctly...; in exclamation; advs ὡς, ἄγαν modify ὀρθὰ, which is an inner acc. (‘bear correct witness’), which can be translated as an adv. in English
355τὸ (ἔ)ργον: his action; nom. subject
355ὡς ἀφροντίστως ἔχει: that (he)..; ind. disc., translate ἔχω, ‘is disposed,’ + adv. as equiv. to εἰμί + pred
357γένος: O race...; voc. dir. address; i.e. sailors
357ναΐας ἀρωγὸν τέχνας: neut. ἀρωγὸν + gen.
359ὃς ἐπέβας: (you) who...; 2s aor. ἐπι-βαίνω
360σέ τοι σέ τοι μόνον: you (as you know), you alone (as you know); emphatic with particle τοι
360δέδορκα: 1s pf. δέρκομαι
360ἐπαρκέσοντ(α): intending to fend off; or ‘going to fend off,’ acc. fut. pple expressing purpose

361ἀλλά: come!; as often before an imperative
361συνδάϊξον: 2s aor. imperative

362κακὸν κακῷ διδοὺς ἄκος: offering evil as a cure for evil; nom. sg. pres. pple δίδωμι, ἄκος is a acc. pred. and dat. ind. obj.
362μὴ…τίθει: do not make (x) (y); τίθε-ε, neg. 2s pres. imperative with a double acc. (obj. and pred.); πλέον, ‘greater’ or ‘more’ is acc. pred.
364ὁρᾷς..μὲ (εἶναι): Do you see that I...(am)?; an extended question with ind. disc.; add infinitive
364τὸν θρασύν, τὸν εὐκάρδιον, τὸν ἄτρεστον: the bold, the stout-hearted, the untrembling...; three substantives in apposition to μέ
365ἐν δαΐοις: among hostiles, among enemies
366ἐν ἀφόβοις...θηρσὶ: among...
366δεινὸν χέρας: terrible in (respect to) my hands; acc. pred. after μὲ εἶναι; acc. of respect
367ὤμοι: Woe is me!; can govern a gen. of cause
367γέλωτος: the mockery!; gen. of cause
367οἷον ὑβρίσθην ἄρα: what sort (of outrage) I suffered then!; in exclamation, 1s aor. pass. ὑβρίζω ‘commit outrage;’ οἷον is an inner acc.
368μή...αὔδα: Don’t...; neg. imperative, αὔδα-ε
368λίσσομαί σ(ὲ): parenthetical

369πόδα: on foot; acc. of respect
371ὦ πρὸς θεῶν: O, by the gods; in exclamation

372ὦ δύσμορος: O wretched (am I); nom. pred.

374μεθῆκα: 1s aor. μεθ-ίημι
374ἐν δ᾽...πεσὼν: falling upon; aor. pple πίπτω

Commentary

376ἔδευσα: 1s aor. δεύω
377τί δῆτ(α) ἂν ἀλγοίης: Why then would…?; potential pres. opt.; δῆτα is resumptive
377ἐπ᾽ ἐξειργασμένοις: for things (already) done; pf. pass. pple and substantive, ἐξ-εργάζομαι; ἐπί + dat. here expresses a motive or reason
378οὐ...γένοιτ(ο) ἂν...ὅπως: it could not be possible...; similar to οὐκ ἔστιν ὅπως, literally ‘there could not come to be a how,’ aor. potential opt.
378ταῦτ(α)…οὐχ ὧδε ἔχειν: that these things not be so; logical subject of γένοιτ(ο); translate ἔχω + adv. as εἰμί + pred.
379πάντ(α) ὁρῶν: (you)...; i.e. Odysseus
380τέκνον Λαρτίου: voc. dir. address
381κακοπινέστατόν...στρατοῦ: in apposition
381ἄλημα: fine-witted knave, wily trickster; from the verb ἀλέω, ‘finely ground flour,’ but used here of Odysseus
382πολὺν γέλωτ(α): acc. obj.
382ὑπ(ὸ) ἡδονῆς: out of...; ὑπό expressing cause
383ξύν...θεῷ: along with god; i.e. the gods determine the outcome
383πᾶς: everyone...; i.e. each one of us in general
383καὶ γελᾷ κ(αὶ ὀ)δύρεται: both...and...; 3s pres.
384ἴδοιμι: Would that..., May I...; opt. of wish, 1s aor. opt. ὁράω; νιν refers to Odysseus
384μὴν: truly, indeed
384καίπερ ὧδ(ε) ἀτώμενος: although...; pres. mid. pple concessive in sense
385ἰώ μοί μοι: Ah me, me!
386μηδὲν μέγ(α) εἴπῃς: Do not...; prohibitive subj. (μή + aor. subj.), 2s aor. λέγω
386μέγ(α): any proud word, any boast; the indefinite ‘any’ comes from μηδὲν
386ἵν(α)…κακοῦ: in what trouble...; κακοῦ is a partitive gen.; 2s pres. εἰμί
387προγόνων: of (my) ancestors
389πῶς ἂν... θάνοιμι: How might I...?; aor. potential opt. θνῄσκω but expressing a wish
390ὀλέσσας: (after)...; nom. sg. aor. pple ὄλλυμι
390βασιλῆς: kings; βασιλέ-ας, i.e. the Atreides

395σκότος, ἐμὸν φάος,

400ἔτ᾽ ἄξιος βλέπειν τιν᾽ εἰς ὄνασιν ἀνθρώπων.
401ἀλλά μ᾽ ἁ Διὸς

403bποῖ τις οὖν φύγῃ;
404ποῖ μολὼν μενῶ;

Commentary

391τέλος: finally, at last; adverbial acc.
391κ(αὶ) αὐτός: I myself also; adverbial καί
391ἂν θάνοιμι: see note on previous page
392ὅταν κατεύχῃ: whenever...; κατεύχη(σ)αι, general temporal clause with ἄν + 2s pres. subj.
392κα(ὶ) ἐμοὶ: for me also; dat. of interest
392θανεῖν: aor. inf. θνῄσκω
393εὔχε(σ)ο: 2s pres. mid. imperative
393τινα εἰς ὄνασιν: for…; expressing purpose
393τί: Why...?
393ζῆν με: that...; ind. disc. with pres. inf. ζάω
393σοῦ τεθνηκότος: gen. abs. with pf. act. pple θνῄσκω; pf. indicates a state
395σκότος: darkness; i.e. of death; dir. address
395ἐμὸν φάος: in apposition
396ἔρεβος: in apposition; ἔρεβος means both ‘darkness’ and is a proper name for the Underworld
396ὡς ἐμοί: for me, at least; ‘as far as for me’
397ἕλεσθέ: choose, take; 2p aor. imper. αἱρέω
397οἰκήτορα: as (your)...; acc. pred.
399οὔτε...θεῶν γένος οὔθ᾽ ἁμερίων...ἀνθρώπων: to either the race of gods or of mortal men; ἡμέριοι is often used substantively for mortals
400ἔτι ἄξιος (εἰμί): I am (no) longer worthy; + complementary inf.
401ἡ...ἀλκίμη θεὸς: i.e. Athena
401Διὸς: (daughter) of Zeus
403ὀλέθρι(α): destructively, fatally; neut. pl. adverbial acc. or fem. pred. adj. as adverb
403bφύγῃ: should flee?, is to flee?; deliberative subj., 3s pres. subj.
404μολὼν: nom. sg. aor. pple βλώσκω
404μενῶ: should I...? Am I to...?; deliberative subj., 1s pres. subj.
405405-8: A number of challenging conjectures
405405-8: A number of challenging conjectures. Please consult a more advanced level commentary for suggested readings
405τὰ μὲν: some (of my affairs); nom. subject
406τοιοῖσδ᾽ ὁμοῦ πέλας: along with these sort near (me); i.e. the victims

Commentary

406τοιοῖσδ᾽ ὁμοῦ πέλας: along with these sort near (me); i.e. the victims
406μώραις δ᾽ ἄγραις προσκείμεθα: and (if) we lie attached to a foolish hunt; a second verb parallel to φθίνει above; dat. of compound verb
407ἄν...φονεύοι: would...; potential opt.
407δίπαλτος: brandishing (spears) in both hands
409χειρὶ: dat. of means
410ὦ δυστάλαινα: O, bad-suffering (am I)
410τοιάδ᾽ ἄνδρα χρήσιμον φωνεῖν: that...; ind. disc., ἄνδρα χρήσιμον is acc. subj.; τοιάδε is acc. obj.
411ἃ...οὗτος...ἔτλη...ἄν (εἰπεῖν): which things this one would...; relative clause with contrary to fact (ἄν + impf. indicative); assume inf.
412bπόροι...ἐπάκτιον: voc., direct address
414bπολὺν πολύν...δαρόν δὴ...χρόνον: for a long, long, quite too long a time; acc. of duration and intensive δή
415κατείχετ(ε): 2p impf.
415ἀμφὶ Τροίαν: around...
415ἀλλ᾽ οὐκέτι μ(ε κατείχετε): assume the verb
416ἀμπνοὰς ἔχοντα: (while)...; i.e. breathing and being alive; pple ἔχω modifying με
416φρονῶν: nom. sg. pres. pple
416ἴστω: let...know; 3rd person imperative οἶδα; τοῦτό is acc. obj.
417ὦ Σκαμάνδριοι...ῥοαί: voc., direct address
420Ἀργείοις: to...; dat. of interest

Αἴ
430αἰαῖ· τίς ἄν ποτ᾽ ᾤεθ᾽ ὧδ᾽ ἐπώνυμον
431τοὐμὸν ξυνοίσειν ὄνομα τοῖς ἐμοῖς κακοῖς;
432νῦν γὰρ πάρεστι καὶ δὶς αἰάζειν ἐμοὶ
433καὶ τρίς· τοιούτοις γὰρ κακοῖς ἐντυγχάνω·

Commentary

421οὐκέτι...μὴ ἴδητ(ε): no longer will you see...; οὐ μὴ + aor. subj. can express an emphatic denial in the future
422ἔπος μέγα: a great boast; ‘a great word’
424ἐξερῶ: 1s fut. ἐξ-ερέω
424οἷον οὔτινα Τροία στρατοῦ δέρχθη: the sort of one whom Troy has not seen among the army; 3s aor. pass. δέρκομαι; στρατοῦ is partitive gen.
425χθονὸς...ἀπὸ Ἑλλανίδος: from...
425μολόντ(α): acc. sg. aor. pple βλώσκω
426ἄτιμος: nom. pred.; translate after verb
427πρόκειμαι: I lie prostrate; a verb used for the setting out of a corpse for burial
428οὔτοι…οὐδ(ε)…ἔχω: I do not know...nor...; ἔχω: I am able; as often + complementary inf.
428σ(ε) ἀπείργειν: (how) to...; inf. ἀπ-είργω
428ὅπως ἐῶ λέγειν: how I am to...; ind. question, deliberative subj. ἐάω
429κακοῖς τοιοῖσδε: with...; dat. of compound verb
429συμπεπτωκότα: pf. act. pple συμ-πίπτω modifying σε
430ἄν ᾤετ(ο): would have thought; contrary to fact with ἄν + impf. mid. οἴομαι
430ἐπώνυμον τὸ ἐμὸν ξυνοίσειν ὄνομα: that my given name...; ind. disc. with fut. inf. συμ-φέρω + dat.; the name Αἴας is similar to αἰαῖ, αἰάζω
432καὶ δὶς…καὶ τρίς: both...and (even)...
432πάρεστι...ἐμοὶ: it is in my power; ‘it is at for me’ + complementary inf.
434ὅτου πατὴρ: (I) whose father...; i.e. Telamon, whom Heracles brought to Troy before the Trojan war
435τὰ πρῶτα καλλιστεῖ(α) ἀριστεύσας: winning...; i.e. Hesione, daughter of the Trojan King Laomedon
435στρατοῦ: of...; partitive gen. after καλλιστεῖα

Commentary

436φέρων: pple, φέρω ‘carry off’ or ‘win’
437ὁ (ἐ)κείνου παῖς: in apposition to ἐγώ
437τὸν αὐτόν: the same; modifying τόπον
438Τροίας: of...; appositional gen. with τόπον
438ἐπελθὼν: aor. pple ἐπ-έρχομαι
438οὐκ ἐλάσσονι σθένει: with...; dat. of manner; σθένεϊ here means ‘force (of men)’; litotes ‘no weaker’
439οὐδ᾽ ἔργα μείο(ν)α: and...no lesser deeds; οὐδέ and comparative adj. μείω form a litotes
439χειρὸς...ἐμῆς: from...; gen. of source
439ἀρκέσας: performing; here with ἔργα μείο(ν)α as inner acc.
440Ἀργείοισιν: by...; dat. of agent with ἄτιμος
440ἀπόλλυμαι: I am perishing; pres. mid.
441τοσοῦτόν γ(ε) ἐξεπίστασθαι: that (I) know this much at least; ind. disc.; γε is restrictive
442εἰ Ἀχιλλεὺς…ἔμελλε, ἄν ἔμαρψεν: if Achilles were going to...; no one would have...; contrary to fact condition
442ζῶν: nom. sg. pres. pple ζάω
442ὅπλων τῶν ὧν πέρι: about...; anastrophe; ὧν is gen. pl. of ἑός
443κράτος ἀριστείας: i.e. the prize of first place
443τινί: to someone; dat. of interest
444ἀντ(ὶ) ἐμοῦ: in place of..., instead of...
445νῦν δ(ὲ): but as it is; often after contrafactual
445φωτὶ παντουργῷ: for a man...; dat. of interest
445φρένας: in his wits; acc. of respect with dat.
446ἔπραξαν: exacted them; i.e. stole them
446ἀνδρὸς τοῦδε…κράτη: the victories of this here man; i.e. of Ajax; neut. pl. κράτεα
447κ(αὶ) εἰ μὴ…ἀπῇξαν, ἄν ἐψήφισαν: if...had not rushed from my plan, they would have voted; contrary to fact
449δίκην κατ(ὰ)…φωτός: a judgment against…
450νῦν δ(ὲ): but as it is; often after contrafactual
450Διὸς: (daughter) of Zeus

451μ(ὲ)…ἔσφηλεν: made me fail, frustrated me; aor. σφάλλω, ‘make fall’

Commentary

466τὸ (ἔ)ργον: the deed
466ἀλλὰ δῆτα: well, then; δῆτα is resumptive; a 2nd option and alternative to πότερα in 460
466ἰὼν: nom. sg. pple ἔρχομαι
467ξυμπεσὼν: falling in with (dat); i.e. fighting; aor. pple συμ-πίπτω + dat. of compound verb

468δρῶν: nom. sg. pple δράω

469ἀλλ᾽ ὧδέ γ(ε): but in this way
469ἂν εὐφράναιμί: I might...; potential opt.
470οὐκ ἔστι ταῦτα: it is not possible in these matters; common impersonal verb, acc. of respect

Commentary

555ἕως...μάθῃς: until...; anticipatory aor. subj. μανθάνω here without the usual ἄν
556ὅπως...δείξεις: that you show...; an object clause (ὅπως + fut. ind., S2211); σε is object
556ὅταν δ᾽ ἵκη(σ)αι: whenever...; general temporal clause with ἄν + 2s aor. ἱκνέομαι
556πατρὸς...ἐν ἐχθροῖς: among...
557οἷος ἐξ οἵου (ἐ)τράφης: what sort of man (and) from what sort you...; ind. question after δείξεις; 2s aor. pass. τρέφω; οἷος is pred. nom.
558βόσκε(σ)ο: 2s pres. mid. imper. + dat. means
558νέαν...ἀτάλλων: fostering your young soul
559χαρμονήν: in apposition with dat. of interest
560οὔτοι μή τις ὑβρίσῃ: Not any...will outrage; οὐ μή + aor. subj. (3s) can express emphatic denial in the future (S1804); partitive Ἀχαιῶν; cf. 421
560οἶδα: parenthetical
561στυγναῖσι λώβαις: with...; dat. of means
561οὐδὲ...ὄντ(α): not even (when)...; acc. pple εἰμί
562Τεῦκρον...λείψω: I will leave Teucer as...; a double acc. (obj. pred.): the rest is acc. pred.
563κ(αὶ) εἰ: even if...; concessive
563τροφέ(α) τ᾽ ἄοκνον ἔμπα: and...; acc. τροφεύς
567ἀγγείλατ(ε): 2p aor. imperative ἀγγέλλω
567ὅπως...δείξει: that he show...; see note for line 556
569Ἐριβοίᾳ λέγω: I mean to Eriboea
570ὥς...γένηται: so that he may...; purpose clause
570σφιν: for them; dat. of interest, pronoun σφεῖς

646ἅπανθ᾽ ὁ μακρὸς κἀναρίθμητος χρόνος
647φύει τ᾽ ἄδηλα καὶ φανέντα κρύπτεται·
648κοὐκ ἔστ᾽ ἄελπτον οὐδέν, ἀλλ᾽ ἁλίσκεται
649χὠ δεινὸς ὅρκος χαἰ περισκελεῖς φρένες.
650κἀγὼ γάρ, ὃς τὰ δείν᾽ ἐκαρτέρουν τότε,
651βαφῇ σίδηρος ὣς ἐθηλύνθην στόμα
652πρὸς τῆσδε τῆς γυναικός· οἰκτίρω δέ νιν
653χήραν παρ᾽ ἐχθροῖς παῖδά τ᾽ ὀρφανὸν λιπεῖν.
654ἀλλ᾽ εἶμι πρός τε λουτρὰ καὶ παρακτίους
655λειμῶνας, ὡς ἂν λύμαθ᾽ ἁγνίσας ἐμὰ
656μῆνιν βαρεῖαν ἐξαλύξωμαι θεᾶς·
657μολών τε χῶρον ἔνθ᾽ ἂν ἀστιβῆ κίχω,
658κρύψω τόδ᾽ ἔγχος τοὐμόν, ἔχθιστον βελῶν,
659γαίας ὀρύξας ἔνθα μή τις ὄψεται·
660ἀλλ᾽ αὐτὸ νὺξ Ἅιδης τε σῳζόντων κάτω.

Commentary

646ἅπαντ(α)…φύει τ᾽ ἄδηλα: brings forth...; i.e. reveals all things previously unseen
647(ἅπαντα) φανέντα: after being shown; after appearing; nom. pl. aor. pass. pple φαίνω
647κρύπτεται: are hidden (again); pass. or mid.
648οὐκ ἔστ(ι)…οὐδέν: there is not anything...
648ἁλίσκεται: are overcome; lit. ‘are caught,’ 3s with 3p subject
649χὠ...χαἰ: both...and...; κ(αὶ) ὁ... κ(αὶ) αἰ
650κα(ὶ ἐ)γὼ γάρ: for I also
650τὰ δείν(ὰ): wondrously, strangely; adverbial acc.
650τότε: at that time
651βαφῇ σίδηρος ὣς: just as iron by dipping in water; i.e. is tempered; clause of comparison
651ἐθηλύνθην: 1s aor. pass.
651στόμα: in...; acc. of respect
652πρὸς τῆσδε τῆς γυναικός: from...
652οἰκτίρω...λιπεῖν: I feel pity to...; aor. λείπω
654εἶμι: 1s fut. ἔρχομαι
654παρ(ὰ) ἐχθροῖς: among..., beside...
655ὡς ἂν...ἐξαλύξωμαι: so that I may...; purpose with aor. subj. (ἄν occurs in poetry)
657μολών: nom. sg. aor. pple βλώσκω
659γαίας...ἔνθα...ὄψεται: (some) earth where...; partitive gen.; relative clause, fut. mid. ὁράω
659ἔνθ(α) ἂν...κίχω: wherever...; general relative clause with 1s aor. subj. κιχάνω
660σῳζόντων: let...keep safe; 3p imperative

661ἐγὼ γὰρ ἐξ οὗ χειρὶ τοῦτ᾽ ἐδεξάμην
662παρ᾽ Ἕκτορος δώρημα δυσμενεστάτου,
663οὔπω τι κεδνὸν ἔσχον Ἀργείων πάρα.
664ἀλλ᾽ ἔστ᾽ ἀληθὴς ἡ βροτῶν παροιμία,
665ἐχθρῶν ἄδωρα δῶρα κοὐκ ὀνήσιμα.
666τοιγὰρ τὸ λοιπὸν εἰσόμεσθα μὲν θεοῖς
667εἴκειν, μαθησόμεσθα δ᾽ Ἀτρείδας σέβειν.
668ἄρχοντές εἰσιν, ὥσθ᾽ ὑπεικτέον. τί μήν;
669καὶ γὰρ τὰ δεινὰ καὶ τὰ καρτερώτατα
670τιμαῖς ὑπείκει· τοῦτο μὲν νιφοστιβεῖς
671χειμῶνες ἐκχωροῦσιν εὐκάρπῳ θέρει·
672ἐξίσταται δὲ νυκτὸς αἰανὴς κύκλος
673τῇ λευκοπώλῳ φέγγος ἡμέρᾳ φλέγειν·
674δεινῶν τ᾽ ἄημα πνευμάτων ἐκοίμισε
675στένοντα πόντον· ἐν δ᾽ ὁ παγκρατὴς ὕπνος

Commentary

661ἐξ οὗ: from which time..., since...
661χειρὶ: in...; dat. place where or means
662παρ᾽ Ἕκτορος...δυσμενεστάτου: from...
663ἔσχον: 1s aor. ἔχω
663Ἀργείων πάρα: from...; anastrophe
665ἐχθρῶν δῶρα (ἐστίν): the gifts of enemies are...; ἐχθρῶν is a subjective gen.
666τὸ λοιπὸν: in the future; acc. of duration
666εἰσόμεσθα: 1p fut. mid. οἶδα
667μαθησόμεσθα: 1p fut. mid. μανθάνω
668ἄρχοντες: leaders; substantive from the pple
668ὥστ(ε) ὑπεικτέον (ἐστίν): so that one must yield; make active this passive construction
668τί μήν;: Why indeed not?; an expression with the force of ‘of course’ or ‘naturally’
669καὶ γὰρ τὰ δεινά: for even things dreadful; neut. pl. subject
670τιμαῖς: to privileges/honors; i.e. of authority
671εὐκάρπῳ θέρει: for...; dat. of interest; i.e. winter yields to summer
672ἐξίσταται: stands out of the way
673τῇ λευκοπώλῳ...ἡμέρᾳ: for...; dat. interest
673φέγγος...φλέγειν: to...; infinitive of purpose
674ἐκοίμισε: gnomic aor.; κοιμίζω as present
675ἐν δ᾽: and among them

676λύει πεδήσας, οὐδ᾽ ἀεὶ λαβὼν ἔχει.
677ἡμεῖς δὲ πῶς οὐ γνωσόμεσθα σωφρονεῖν;
678ἔγωγ᾽· ἐπίσταμαι γὰρ ἀρτίως ὅτι
679ὅ τ᾽ ἐχθρὸς ἡμῖν ἐς τοσόνδ᾽ ἐχθαρτέος,
680ὡς καὶ φιλήσων αὖθις, ἔς τε τὸν φίλον
681τοσαῦθ᾽ ὑπουργῶν ὠφελεῖν βουλήσομαι,
682ὡς αἰὲν οὐ μενοῦντα· τοῖς πολλοῖσι γὰρ
683βροτῶν ἄπιστός ἐσθ᾽ ἑταιρείας λιμήν.
684ἀλλ᾽ ἀμφὶ μὲν τούτοισιν εὖ σχήσει· σὺ δὲ
685ἔσω θεοῖς ἐλθοῦσα διὰ τάχους, γύναι,
686εὔχου τελεῖσθαι τοὐμὸν ὧν ἐρᾷ κέαρ.
687ὑμεῖς δ᾽, ἑταῖροι, ταὐτὰ τῇδέ μοι τάδε
688τιμᾶτε, Τεύκρῳ τ᾽, ἢν μόλῃ, σημήνατε
689μέλειν μὲν ἡμῶν, εὐνοεῖν δ᾽ ὑμῖν ἅμα.
690ἐγὼ γὰρ εἶμ᾽ ἐκεῖσ᾽ ὅποι πορευτέον·

Commentary

676λύει πεδήσας: (after) binding (someone), releases (him); same object aorist participle and verb
676λαβὼν ἔχει: (after) grabbing (someone), does hold him; same object aorist participle and verb
677γνωσόμεσθα: 1st plural future middle γιγνώσκω
678ὅτι…(ἔστίν) ἐχθαρτέος: that he must be hated; “is to be hated” + dative of agent (S1488)
679ἐς τοσόνδε: only to the extent; “this much”
680ὡς καὶ φιλήσων αὖθις: that he in fact will be friend; ὡς + future participle of alleged cause or purpose (S2086)
680ἔς τε τὸν φίλον: and in regard to a friend
681τοσαῦτ(α): only so much; inner accusative
681βουλήσομαι: future middle
682ὡς αἰὲν οὐ μενοῦντα: that he will not always remain a friend; future participle; see note for line 680
682τοῖς πολλοῖσι...βροτῶν: to most mortals; dative of reference
683ἄπιστός...ἑταιρείας λιμήν: the haven of comradeship is not trustworthy
684ἀμφὶ...τούτοισιν: concerning these things
684εὖ σχήσει: it will be well; future ἔχω, where ἔχω + adverb is equivalent to εἰμί + predicate adjective
684σὺ δέ: i.e. Tecmessa, in reply to μέν above
685θεοῖς...εὔχε(σ)ο: present imperative; dative indirect object
685διὰ τάχους: with speed; τάχεος, genitive of τάχος
686τὸ (ἐ)μὸν ὧν ἐρᾷ κέαρ: what my heart desires; relative with implied antecedent; 3rd singular present ἐράω
687τῇδέ: as this one; dative special adjective αὐτός (S1500)
687μοι: I beg you, please; ethical dative
687τὰ αὐτὰ τάδε: these same things
688σημήνατε μέλειν...εὐνοεῖν: tell Teucer to care for us and be kind to you all at the same time
688ἢν μόλῃ: if he comes; 3rd singular aorist subjunctive βλώσκω; future more vivid condition
690ἔγωγ(ε): I for my part (will learn)
690πορευτέον: I must go; literally “it is to be traveled”

726τοῦ μανέντος: of the one driven mad, i.e. Ajax; aorist passive deponent participle μαίνομαι; genitive of possession with ξύναιμον
726κα(ὶ ἐ)πιβουλευτοῦ στρατοῦ: and plotter against the army; the dative object στρατῷ is attracted into the genitive
727ἀποκαλοῦντες: calling him; participle governs a double accusative
727ὡς οὐκ ἀρκέσοι: saying that he would not fend off; indirect discourse, future optative replacing future indicative

811χωρῶμεν, ἐγκονῶμεν: Let us...; 1p hortatory subj.
811οὐχ ἕδρας ἀκμὴ: (it is) not time for sitting; ἀκμὴ, ‘point,’ is often a synonym for καιρός
812θέλοντας: (we) wanting...; acc. pple (ἐ)θέλω; the relationship with the previous line is unclear
812σπεύδῃ: hastens; 3s subj. + aor. inf. θνῄσκω
813ἕτοιμος (ἐιμί): (I am)...; + explanatory inf.

815ὁ σφαγεὺς: i.e. a sacrificial knife, not Ajax
815ἕστηκεν: stands; pf. ἵστημι denotes a state:
815τομώτατος: the sharpest
816(ἐστίν) τῳ: (there is) for one; or ‘one has,’ dat. of possession; alternate form for indef. τινι
816καὶ λογίζεσθαι: even to consider it
817ξένων: among guest-friends; partitive
818μισηθέντος: gen. sg. aor. pass. ppe μισέω
818ὁρᾶν: to look upon; explanatory inf.
819πέπηγε: it sticks; pf. πήγνυμι
821ἔπηξα: I stuck; aor. πήγνυμι
821περιστείλας: wrapping it around (in earth)
822θανεῖν: to die; inf. of purpose
824εἰκός: (it is) reasonable
824ἄρκεσον: help; aor. imperative ἀρκέω
825οὐ λόγῳ...μόνον·: not in words alone; dat. of means and adverbial acc.; in contrast to ἔργου
825λαχεῖν: to obtain; aor. inf. λαγχάνω

826πέμψον τιν᾽ ἡμῖν ἄγγελον, κακὴν φάτιν
827Τεύκρῳ φέροντα, πρῶτος ὥς με βαστάσῃ
828πεπτῶτα τῷδε περὶ νεορράντῳ ξίφει,
829καὶ μὴ πρὸς ἐχθρῶν του κατοπτευθεὶς πάρος
830ῥιφθῶ κυσὶν πρόβλητος οἰωνοῖς θ᾽ ἕλωρ.
831τοσαῦτά σ᾽, ὦ Ζεῦ, προστρέπω, καλῶ δ᾽ ἅμα
832πομπαῖον Ἑρμῆν χθόνιον εὖ με κοιμίσαι,
833ξὺν ἀσφαδάστῳ καὶ ταχεῖ πηδήματι
834πλευρὰν διαρρήξαντα τῷδε φασγάνῳ.

836ἀεί θ᾽ ὁρώσας πάντα τἀν βροτοῖς πάθη,
837σεμνὰς Ἐρινῦς τανύποδας, μαθεῖν ἐμὲ
838πρὸς τῶν Ἀτρειδῶν ὡς διόλλυμαι τάλας,
839καί σφας κακοὺς κάκιστα καὶ πανωλέθρους
840ξυναρπάσειαν, ὥσπερ εἰσορῶσ᾽ ἐμὲ

Commentary

826πέμψον: aor. imperative
826ἡμῖν: for me; ethical dat.: ‘please,’ ‘I beg you’
827φέροντα: pres. pple modifying ἄγγελον
827πρῶτος ὥς με βαστάσῃ: so that he may be the first to lift me; purpose clause with 3s aor. subj.
828πεπτῶτα: acc. pf. pple πίπτω with με
828τῷδε περὶ νεορράντῳ ξίφει: around...; a body, when impaled, is around the sword
829καὶ μὴ...ῥιφθῶ: and so that I may not be...; a neg. purpose clause with 1s aor. pass. ῥίπτω
829πρὸς...του: by one of (my) enemies; gen. of source and partitive; alternative form for τινός
829κατοπτευθεὶς: nom. sg. aor. pass. pple
830κυσὶν…οἰωνοῖς τ(ε): for...; dat. pl. of interest
830πρόβλητος: thrown out; pred. adj., translate after ῥιφθῶ (e.g. ‘cast thrown out’)
830ἕλωρ: as prey; a pred. nom.
831τοσαῦτά: so much; adv. acc. (inner acc.)
832πομπαῖον...χθόνιον: this epithet refers to Hermes as the guide of souls to the Underworld
832εὖ με κοιμίσαι: to...; complementary aor. inf.
834διαρρήξαντα: aor. pple δια-ρρήγνυμι
835ἀρωγοὺς τὰς ἀεί τε παρθένους: the eternal maidens as helpers; pred. acc. and acc. obj.
836ὁρώσας: acc. pl. pres. pple ὁράω
836τ(ὰ ἐ)ν βροτοῖς πάθε-α,: sufferings in mortals
837σεμνὰς Ἐρινῦς...: in apposition to παρθένους
837μαθεῖν ἐμὲ ὡς διόλλυμαι: to learn how I am destroyed by the Atreides; proleptic acc.
839κάκιστα: most wretchedly; superlative adv.
840ξυναρπάσειαν: May they seize; opt. of wish
840ὥσπερ: just as...; cl. of comparison; 3p pres.

Χο

Χο
906τίνος ποτ᾽ ἆρ᾽ ἔπραξε χειρὶ δύσμορος;
Τέκ
907αὐτὸς πρὸς αὑτοῦ, δῆλον· ἐν γάρ οἱ χθονὶ
910πηκτὸν τόδ᾽ ἔγχος περιπετὲς κατηγορεῖ.
Χο
911ὤμοι ἐμᾶς ἄτας, οἶος ἄρ᾽ αἱμάχθης, ἄφαρκτος φίλων·
912ἐγὼ δ᾽ ὁ πάντα κωφός, ὁ πάντ᾽ ἄϊδρις, κατημέλησα. πᾷ πᾷ
914κεῖται ὁ δυστράπελος, δυσώνυμος Αἴας;
Τέκ
915οὔτοι θεατός· ἀλλά νιν περιπτυχεῖ

Commentary

901τόνδε συνναύταν: i.e. the chorus itself, who traveled by ship to Troy with Ajax
901τάλας: Wretched (am I)
902ὦ ταλαίφρων γύναι: voc. dir. address
905ὡς ὧδε τοῦδ᾽ ἔχοντος: Since this is so; ‘on the grounds of this being so,’ ὡς + pple (here, gen. abs.) expresses alleged cause; ἔχω (‘be disposed’) + adv. is equiv. to εἰμί + pred.
905αἰάζειν: an allusion to Ajax; Ajax admits that his name corresponds to αἰάζω in lines 430-2
905πάρα: it is possible; πάρα is often a shortened form for πάρ-εστιν ‘be at hand or be possible’ compare the accent on the preposition παρά
906τίνος...χειρὶ: By whose...?; gen. of possession and dat. of means
906ἆρ᾽: ἄρα
906ἔπραξε: aor. πράσσω, ‘do or accomplish (it)’
907οἱ...πηκτὸν: stuck by him; dat. of agent from 3rd person reflexive pronoun ἔ, ‘himself/herself’
907αὐτὸς πρὸς (ἑ)αυτοῦ: he himself by himself; intensive and reflexive pronouns; πρὸς + gen. is gen. of source that often expresses agency
907δῆλόν (ἐστιν): (it is) clear; often translated as an adverb: ‘clearly’
907ἐν...χθονὶ: dat. place where
910περιπετὲς: fallen around; i.e. on which Ajax was impaled; neut. modifying nom. τόδε ἔγχος
910κατηγορεῖ: indicates (it); i.e. that Ajax committed suicide
911ὤμοι...: Alas for + gen. of cause
911οἶος: alone; note the accent
911ἄρ(α): it seems, it turns out, then
911αἱμάχθης: 2s aor. pass. αἱμάσσω
911φίλων: by friends; gen. separation
912ἐγὼ (εἰμί): I(am) + nom. pred.
912πάντα: altogether, entirely; adv. acc. or ac. of respect, ‘in all respects’
912κατημέλησα: 1s aor. κατ-αμελέω
912πᾷ: Where?; πῇ
914δυσώνυμος: cf. line
915θεατός (ἐστιν): he must be seen; ‘(he is) to be seen’ verbal adj. + ἐστίν often expresses necessity or obligation

Commentary

916φάρει...τῷδε: dat. of means; Tecmessa’s
916ἐπεὶ ἄν...τλαίη: since...could...; 3s potential opt. τλάω
917καὶ: actually, in fact; adverbial καί
917βλέπειν: assume αὐτόν, ‘him,’ as obj.
918φυσῶντα… μελανθὲν αἷμα: blowιng...; pple modifying the obj. of βλέπειν; αἷμα is the obj.
918ἄνω πρὸς ῥῖνας: up to his nostrils
919οἰκείας: his own; or ‘the self-inflicted’
920τί δράσω: What am I...?; deliberative subj., 1s aor. subj. δράω
920τίς...βαστάσῃ: who is to...; deliberative subj., 3s aor. subj.
920φίλων: partitive gen.
922ὡς ἀκμαῖ(α): How timely...!; in exclamation, ἀκμαῖα is an adv. acc.
922ἄν, εἰ βαίη, μόλοι: he would..., if he should...; fut. less vivid condition (εἰ opt., ἄν opt.); 3s aor. opt. βαίνω and aor. opt. βλώσκω
923πεπτῶτα: fallen; pf. act. pple πίπτω
923συγκαθαρμόσαι: to...; aor. inf. of purpose
924οἷος ὢν οἵως ἔχεις: In what state you are, though being such a man!; ἔχω (‘be disposed’) + adv. is equiv. to εἰμί + pred.; οἷος is the nom. pred. of ὢν which is the pple of εἰμί concessive in sense
925ὡς...ἄξιος: How worthy...!; in exclamation
925καὶ παρ᾽ ἐχθροῖς: even before...; adverbial καί; i.e. before the Atreides and Odysseus
925τυχεῖν: to obtain + partitive gen.; explanatory (epexegetical) aor. inf. τυγχάνω
926ἔμελλες: “you were intending”; χρόνῳ: dat. of time when
927ἄρα: it turns out, it seems; expressing a truth just realized
930μοῖραν ἀπειρεσίων πόνων: fate/share of limitless toils

1006δυνατόν: is it possible?; μολεῖν is aorist infinitive βλώσκω

Commentary

1021τοιαῦτα μὲν κατ᾽ οἶκον: such things will be at home

1024πικροῦ...κνώδοντος: from...; gen. separation; the sword piercing through the back of Ajax

1026ὡς…ἔμελλέ: that...; ind. disc., Ajax’s sword was given to him by the enemy Hector

1026ἐξέπνευσας: 2s aor. ἐκ-πνέω
1026εἶδες: 2s aor. ὁράω
1026χρόνῳ: in time
1027καὶ θανὼν: even (though) dying; aor. pple θνῇσκω concessive in sense
1028πρὸς θεῶν: by the gods; in exclamation
1028δυοῖν βροτοῖν: dual gen.

1029τοῦδε…πάρα,: from this one; i.e. Ajax
1030ζωστῆρι πρισθεὶς: gripped by this belt; nom. aor. pass. pple πρίω and dat. of means

1093οὐκ ἄν ποτ᾽, ἄνδρες, ἄνδρα θαυμάσαιμ᾽ ἔτι,
1094ὃς μηδὲν ὢν γοναῖσιν εἶθ᾽ ἁμαρτάνει,
1095ὅθ᾽ οἱ δοκοῦντες εὐγενεῖς πεφυκέναι

Commentary

1081ὅπου παρῇ: whenever it is possible; general temporal clause
1081ἃ βούλεται: whatever he wishes; relative clause with implied antecedent
1082ταύτην τὴν πόλιν...πεσεῖν: that this city will sink; indirect discourse with future infinitive πίπτω
1083ἐξ οὐρίων δραμοῦσαν: rushing under favorable winds; aorist participle τρέχω, with the city compared to a ship
1084ἑστάτω: let it be established; 3rd singular perfect imperative ἵστημι
1084καὶ δέος τι καίριον: a certain timely fear also
1085μὴ δοκῶμεν: let us not think; 1st plural hortatory subjunctive
1085δρῶντες: doing; present participle δράω
1085ἃν ἡδώμεθα: whatever we enjoy; general relative clause with ἄν + subjunctive
1086οὐκ ἀντιτίσειν: that we will not pay back; future infinitive in indirect discourse
1086ἃν λυπώμεθα: whatever pains us; general relative clause
1087ἕρπει ταῦτα: these things come
1087οὗτος: this one, i.e. Ajax
1088μέγ᾽ αὖ φρονῶ: I in turn have great thoughts, feel pride
1089ὅπως μὴ...πέσῃς: lest you fall; fearing clause
1089τόνδε μὴ θάπτειν: that you not bury this man
1091μὴ...γένῃ: do not become; prohibitive subjunctive
1091ὑποστήσας: nominative singular aorist participle ὑφίστημι
1092ἐν θανοῦσιν: among the dead; dative plural participle
1093ἄν θαυμάσαιμι: I would wonder; aorist potential optative
1094μηδὲν ὢν γοναῖσιν: being nothing by birth; dative of respect
1095οἱ δοκοῦντες εὐγενεῖς πεφυκέναι: those who seem to be well-born; perfect infinitive φύω

1111τι: at all, in any way; adverbial accusative

1115πλείους: plural from πλέων, more, not πλέως

1116τὸν στρατηγόν: the general, i.e. Agamemnon

1117οἷός περ εἶ: the very sort who you are; περ intensive
1118ἐν κακοῖς: among troubles
1119κἂν ὑπέρδικ᾽ ᾖ: even if they are more than just; present subjunctive εἰμί with neuter plural subject
1120οὐ σμικρὸν φρονεῖν: to have no small thoughts, i.e. to be proud/arrogant
1122μέγ᾽ ἄν τι: something great; inner accusative
1122ἄν κομπάσειας, εἰ λάβοις: you would boast, if you should take; future less vivid condition

1124ὡς δεινόν: how terrible; exclamation
1125ξὺν τῷ δικαίῳ: with justice on one’s side
1125μέγα φρονεῖν: to have big thoughts, to feel pride

1129σεσωσμένος: since...; perfect passive σῴζω, perhaps causal in sense

1131εἰ...οὐκ ἐᾷς: if...; 2s present ἐάω, allow/let

1131παρών: by...; participle πάρειμι causal in sense
1132τούς γ᾽ αὐτὸς αὑτοῦ πολεμίους: yes, I myself do not allow you to bury my own enemies; ellipsis with intensive/reflexive pronouns
1132αὑτοῦ: reflexive, here equivalent to ἑμαυτοῦ

1133σοὶ: before you; dative of compound verb
1133πολέμιος: as an enemy; nominative predicate
1134(με) μισοῦντα (αὐτὸν): present participle μισέω
1134ἐμίσει: imperfect μισέω; assume Ajax as subject
1134ἠπίστασο: 2s imperfect ἐπίσταμαι

1135γὰρ..ηὑρέθης: yes, for...; aorist passive εὑρίσκω

Commentary

1261ὅστις...λέξει: who...; alternative fut. λέγω. τὰ σά: your matters, your case; as an advocate
1262σοῦ...λέγοντος: gen. abs. ἂν μάθοιμ(ι): I would...; potential aor. opt.
1263τὴν βάρβαρον γλῶσσαν: Teucer’s mother is Hesione, captured from the Trojans
1265τούτου: than...; gen. of comparison. σφῷν: to you two; dual dat. ind. obj. ἔχω: I am able; + aor. inf. φράζω
1266τοῦ θανόντος...χάρις: gratitude for...; nom. subj. and objective gen. (aor. pple θνῄσκω). βροτοῖς: for...; dat. interest or compound. προδοῦσ(α): nom. aor. pple προ-δίδωμι; nom. pred.: translate after the following verb
1266ὡς ταχεῖά: How swiftly...! in exclamation, a nom. pred. is often translated as an adv
1268εἴθ(ε)…νοῦς γένοιτο: If only the senses happened to + inf.; ‘Would that...’ expressing unattained opt. of wish: 3s aor. opt. γίγνομαι. ὑμὶν ἀμφοῖν: dual dat. of interest or possession
1268ὅδ(ε) ἁνὴρ: i.e. Agamemnon. οὐδ(ὲ) ἐπὶ σμικρῶν λόγων: not even in brief words; οὐδέ is adverbial
1269ἴσχει μνῆστιν: keeps remembrance, retains memory; with σοῦ above as objective gen. οὗ...προύκαμες: for whom you...; relative clause aor. προ-κάμνω governs a gen.
1270δόρε-ι: with...; dat. of means with the pple
1271οἴχεται δὴ: are just gone; or ‘gone now,’ δὴ can be temporal or intensive with the verb. ἐρριμμένα: pf. pass. ῥίπτω, ‘throw (away)’
1272ὦ...λέξας: O (you) speaking...; aor. pple
1273οὐ...οὐκέτ᾽ οὐδέν: not...any longer at all; οὐδέν is adv. acc. (inner: ‘have no memory’)
1275(ἐντός) ἑρκέων: within the walls. ἐγκεκλῃμένους: pf. pass. ἐγ-κλείω
1275τὸ μηδὲν: being nothing; i.e. useless. ἐν τροπῇ δορὸς: in the turn of the battle

Commentary

1276ἐρρύσατ(ο): rescued; 3s aor. mid. ῥύομαι. μοῦνος: μόνος in an emphatic position at the end. ἀμφὶ μὲν νεῶν...ἑδωλίοις: already around the tops of the ships and naval sterns; in abl. abs.
1278πυρὸς φλέγοντος: gen. abs. with ἀμφὶ. εἰς δὲ ναυτικὰ σκάφεα: toward...; neut. pl.
1279πηδῶντος ἄρδην Ἕκτορος: gen. abs. τάφρων ὕπερ: over...; anastrophe.
1280τίς...ἀπεῖρξεν: who...?; 3s aor. ἀπ-είργω. οὐχ ὅδε ἦν...: Was this one not...?; a question. ὁ δρῶν τάδε: the one doing this; nom. pred., δράω.
1281ὃν...φής βῆναι: who...stepped...; relative; ind. disc. with 2s φημί and aor. inf. βαίνω. οὗ σὺ μή: where you were not; relative adv. οὗ. ποδί: on foot; dat. of means, πούς.
1282ἆρ(α): begins a question; elsewhere equivalent to ἄρα. ἔνδικα: justly; pred. adj. often translated as adv.
1283κ(αὶ ὄ)τ(ε)...ἦλθ(ε): and when he came... Ἕκτορος...μόνου: partitive gen. obj. of λαχών.
1285οὐ...καθείς: casting as his lot in the middle not a ‘runaway,’ a clump of moist dirt; in drawing lots, some would use a lot-token made of dirt to stick to the bottom, so it would not be picked.
1286ὃς...ἔμελλε: which...; his lot jumps out easily. εὐλόφου κυνῆς: from...; where lots are shaken.
1288σὺν δ᾽: and with him; παρών is pres. pple πάρ-ειμι.

1290ποῖ βλέπων: Looking where in the world...? αὐτὰ...θροεῖς: do you actually say these things?

Commentary

1306οὓς...ὠθεῖς ἀθάπτους: whom you push out unburied; relative; ἀθάπτους is pred. acc.
1307ἐπαισχύνε(σ)αι: 2s pres. ἐπ-αισχύνομαι. λέγων: by saying; pres. pple causal in sense.
1308ἴσθι: sg. imperative οἶδα. εἰ βαλεῖτέ που, βαλεῖτε κ(αὶ) ἠμᾶς: if you cast him out anywhere, you will be casting out us also; emotional future more vivid (εἰ fut., fut.).
1310ἐπεὶ καλόν (ἐστιν): since it is right; impersonal verb with dat. of interest. τοῦδ᾽...θανεῖν...γυναικός: to die while working on behalf of this one rather than on behalf of your wife.
1312ἢ τοῦ σοῦ γ᾽ ὁμαίμονος λέγω;: or do I mean your brother’s wife? i.e. Menelaus’.
1313πρὸς ταῦτ(α): in response to these things. ὅρα: consider; sg. imperative. τὸ (ἐ)μόν: my own matters; καί: also.
1314ὡς εἴ με πημανεῖς τι, βουλήσε(σ)αι: since if you harm me at all, you will wish; emotional future more vivid (εἰ fut., fut.).
1315καί: in fact, actually. (ἐ)ν ἐμοί: upon me.
1316καιρὸν: at the right time; adv. acc. ἴσθ(ι): sg. imperative οἶδα. ἐληλυθώς: that you...; ind. disc. with pf. ἔρχομαι, attracted into the nom. of the main verb.
1317ξυνάψων: intending to help tie up, as if a knot; fut. pple expressing purpose. συλλύσων: intending to resolve. πάρει: you are present; 2s πάρ-ειμι.
1319τῷδ᾽ ἐπ᾽ ἀλκίμῳ νεκρῷ: over this valiant dead man.
1320οὐ κλύοντές ἐσμεν: yes, for are we not listening to...? 1p εἰμί + pple equivalent to κλύομεν.

1332ἄκουέ νυν. τὸν ἄνδρα τόνδε πρὸς θεῶν
1333μὴ τλῇς ἄθαπτον ὧδ᾽ ἀναλγήτως βαλεῖν·

Commentary

1321τοῦδ᾽ ὑπ(ὸ) ἀνδρός: from this man.
1322ποίους: which sort? assume λόγους. ἀνδρί: for a man; dat. of interest. συγγνώμην ἔχω: I have forgiveness; an idiom.
1323κλύοντι φλαῦρα: after hearing low words; pres. pple modifying ἀνδρί. συμβαλεῖν ἔπεα κακά: to join in throwing troubling words.
1324δρῶν: doing (x) to (y); a double acc. ἦν: 3s impf. εἰμί.
1325τί γάρ σ᾽ ἔδρασεν: What in fact did he do to you? aor. δράω. ὥστε...(σε) ἔχειν: so that you have...; result clause; καί is adverbial.
1326φησ(ι): 3s pres. φημί, i.e. Teucer. οὐ...ἐάσειν: that he will not let alone; ind. disc. fut. inf. ἐάω.
1327ἀλλὰ...θάψειν: but that he will bury; second ind. disc. with fut. inf. θάπτω. πρὸς βίαν...ἐμοῦ: in defiance of me; ἐμοῦ is objective gen.
1328ἔξεστιν: Is it possible...? impersonal. εἰπόντι...φίλῳ: for a friend to speak; dat. of interest and aor. pple λέγω. τἀληθῆ: the truth.
1329σοί: dat. ind. object of εἰπόντι. μηδὲν ἧσσον ἢ: no less than; μηδέν is an adverbial acc., and ἧσσον is a comparative adv.
1330εἴπ(ε): speak; aor. imperative. ἦ γάρ: for otherwise, for truly. εἴην οὐκ ἂν: I would not be; potential opt. εἰμί.
1330ἐπεὶ...νέμω: since I consider...; νέμω can mean ‘hold’ or ‘hold in mind.’
1332πρὸς θεῶν: by the gods!; in exclamation.
1333μὴ τλῇς: Do not dare...; prohibitive subj. μή + aor. subj. τλάω.
1333μηδὲ νικησάτω: nor let...; 3s aor. imperative. μηδαμῶς: in any way; positive after μηδέ.
1335τοσόνδε μισεῖν: to hate so much; complementary inf. ὥστε τὴν δίκην πατεῖν: so as to trample justice; result.

1343οὐ γάρ τι τοῦτον, ἀλλὰ τοὺς θεῶν νόμους
1344φθείροις ἄν. ἄνδρα δ᾽ οὐ δίκαιον, εἰ θάνοι,

1349μὴ χαῖρ᾽, Ἀτρείδη, κέρδεσιν τοῖς μὴ καλοῖς.

1350τόν τοι τύραννον εὐσεβεῖν οὐ ῥᾴδιον.

Commentary

1336κ(αὶ ἐ)μοί: to me also; dat. of reference. ἦν οὗτος: this one was; 3s impf. εἰμί.
1337ἐξ οὗ: from which time, since. (ἐ)κράτησα: I prevailed over; i.e. gained.
1338ἔγωγε: yes, I do. ἐμίσουν δέ: but I hated him; 1s impf. μισέω. ἦν καλόν: it was right; impersonal.
1338ὄντ(α)...τοιόνδε: although being such; pple εἰμί concessive in sense modifying αὐτόν. μοι: toward me; dat. interest with τοιόνδε.
1339ἀντατιμάσαιμι ἄν: I would dishonor in return; potential opt., 1s aor. ὥστε μὴ λέγειν: so as to deny, say that...not; result clause.
1339ὥστε: so that, as a result. ἂν...ἀτιμάζοιτο: he would be dishonored; potential opt., 3s pres. passive. σοι: by you; dat. of agent.
1340ἕν(α) ἄνδρ(α) (εἶναι) ἄριστον Ἀργείων: that one man was the best of the Argives, i.e. Ajax. ἰδεῖν: to look upon; explanatory inf. with ἄριστον.
1340ὅσοι...ἀφικόμεσθα: as many of us as arrived; relative clause with Ἀργείων as antecedent.
1343τι: at all, in any way; adv. acc.
1344φθείροις ἄν: you would destroy; potential opt. ἄνδρα...τὸν ἐσθλόν: single obj. of the inf. βλάπτειν; it is also possible to take τὸν ἐσθλόν as acc. subj. and ἄνδρα as object.
1345οὐδ᾽ ἐὰν μισῶν κυρῇς: not even if you happen to hate him; 2s aor. subj. in a future more vivid condition; κυρέω takes a complementary pple.
1346ταῦτα: in this way; adv. acc. τοῦδε: for this one, with the prefix ὑπερ-. ἐμοί: against me; dat. of interest.
1348θανόντι καί: on someone even after death; dat. of compound verb. προσεμβῆναί σε: that you trample additionally; ind. disc., aor. inf.
1349μὴ χαῖρ(ε): do not rejoice in + dat. cause.
1350οὐ ῥᾴδιον (ἐστίν): it is not easy; impersonal.

Commentary

1351εὖ λέγουσι...νέμειν (ῥᾴδιον ἐστίν): but (it is easy) to give honor to friends speaking well; i.e. Agamemnon is doing Odysseus a favor.
1352τῶν ἐν τέλει: those in command, those in office; gen. of source, obj. of κλύειν.
1353παῦσαι: aor. imperative. κρατεῖς: you prevail. τῶν φίλων: by...; lit. from..., gen. of source. νικώμενος: if convinced; pres. passive pple.
1355ἦν: 3s impf. εἰμί.
1356ποήσεις: 2s fut. ποιέω. αἰδέε(σ)αι: do you feel shame before; or show respect to; 2s pres. mid. αἰδέομαι.
1357μέμνησ(ο): 2s pf. mid. imperative μιμνήσκω. ὁποίῳ φωτὶ τὴν χάριν δίδως: to what sort of man...; indirect question; 2s pres. δίδωμι with dat. indirect object.
1357γάρ: yes, for...; or in fact with 3s pres. τῆς ἔχθρας πολύ: more than hostility; adv. acc. and gen. of comparison.
1358τοιοίδε...φῶτες (εἰσίν): however, such men (are)...; Jebb suggests τοιοίδε refers to Odysseus, others to Ajax. ἔμπληκτοι: nom. pred. βροτῶν: among..., partitive gen.
1359ἦ κάρτα πολλοὶ (εἰσίν): indeed... νῦν...καὶ αὖθις: now...and later...; nom. pred.; i.e. at one time and then at another.
1360(με) τοιούσδ᾽...κτᾶσθαι φίλους: that I...; indirect discourse with pres. mid. inf. κτάομαι, governed by ἐπαινεῖς; i.e. friends such as Ajax. ἐπαινεῖς: you approve, you recommend.
1361φιλῶ: I like + complementary infinitive.
1362τῇδε τ(ῇ) ἡμέρᾳ: on this day; dat. of time when. φανεῖς: you will show (x) (y); fut. φαίνω governs a double acc. (obj., pred.).
1363ἄνδρας ἐνδίκους: (I will show you) just men. Ἕλλησι πᾶσιν: to...; dat. of reference.
1364με...ἐᾶν: that...; indirect discourse, inf. ἐάω, allow.
1365ἵξομαι: fut. ἱκνέομαι; i.e. I too will need it.

Commentary

1367τῷ...μᾶλλον ἢ (ἐ)μαυτῷ: For whom...more than...? τῷ is alternative to τίνι, dat. sg. τίς. με...πονεῖν: that I...; indirect discourse. (ἐστίν) εἰκός: is it reasonable; impersonal.
1368τὸ (ἔ)ργον: nom. subject; σὸν and ἐμὸν are predicates. ἆρα: then; ἆρα = ἄρα. κεκλήσεται: fut. pass. καλέω with nom. pred.
1369ὡς (ἐ)ὰν ποήσῃς,...ἔσῃ: since if you do, you will...; fut. more vivid condition (ἐάν + subj., fut.) with 2s aor. subj. ποιέω and 2s fut. εἰμί; ὡς here suggests cause or purpose.
1369πάντ(α) ὅμοια: in...; acc. of respect. (ἑ)αυτῷ: for himself; dat. of interest.
1370ὡς...νέμοιμ(ι) ἂν: (namely) that...would give; indirect discourse in apposition to τοῦτο; potential opt. τῆσδε: than...; gen. of comparison, i.e. χάρις. καὶ μείζο(ν)α: even greater; adv. and acc. sg.
1372οὗτος: i.e. Ajax. κα(ὶ) ἐκεῖ κα(ὶ ἐ)νθάδε: both there and here; i.e. among the living and among the dead. ὢν: nom. pres. pple εἰμί.
1373ἀλλ(ὰ)...μέντοι: Well,...certainly. εὖ γε: very well; emphatic γε. τοῦτ(ο) ἐπίστασ(ο): pres. imperative ἐπίσταμαι.
1373ἔσται: fut. εἰμί. ἔξεστ(ι): it is possible. ἃ χρῇς: what you desire; relative clause with missing antecedent as object of δράω; χρῇς is a defective verb found only in 2s and 3s.
1374μὴ λέγει: denies; or says that...not. σ(ε)...σοφὸν φῦναι: that you...; indirect discourse with aor. inf. φύω, is/are (lit. grow to be), governed by μὴ λέγει. γνώμῃ: in judgment; dat. of respect.
1375τοιοῦτον ὄντα: although being this sort of man, i.e. wise; concessive in sense.
1376καὶ...γε: emphasizes what is between them. τὸ ἀπὸ τοῦδε: from this moment.
1377ὅσον τότ᾽ ἐχθρὸς ἦ τοσόνδ᾽ εἶναι φίλος: that I am a friend as much as I was once an enemy; indirect discourse, literally by as much as...by this much, adv. acc. (extent by degree).
1378τὸν θανόντα τόνδε: i.e. Ajax, object of the infinitive.
1379μηδὲν...ὅσων: none of the things which...; acc. relative attracted into gen.

Commentary

1381ἄριστ(ε) Ὀδυσσεῦ: voc. direct address. πάντ(α): in every way; adv. acc. ἔχω: I am able + aor. inf.
1382λόγοισι: because of your words; dat. of cause. ἐλπίδος πολύ: more than expectation; comparative adv. and gen. of comparison; i.e. more than I expected.
1383τούτῳ: to this one, i.e. Ajax; dat. interest. ὢν: although/while; concessive pple εἰμί.
1384μόνος: you alone; modifying the 2s subject. παρέστης: 2s aor. παρ-ίστημι, stand beside. χερσίν: with helping hands; dat. pl. χείρ. ἔτλης: 2s aor. τλάω + complementary aor. inf. παρών: while present; pres. pple.
1385θανόντι τῷδε: over this dead man; dat. of compound verb, aor. pple θνῄσκω. ζῶν: while living; pres. pple ζάω. μέγα: greatly; adv. acc.
1386ὡς...ἠθελησάτην: just as...; clause of comparison with dual aor. ἐθέλω. ὁ (ἐ)πιβρόντητος: adj. in attributive position modifying ὁ στρατηγός. μολών: nom. aor. pple βλώσκω.
1388αὐτόν: i.e. Ajax. ἐκβαλεῖν: aor. inf. ἐκ-βάλλω. ταφῆς ἄτερ: ἄτερ + gen. object.
1389σφε: them, acc. pl.; i.e. the Atreidae. ὁ πατὴρ...φθείρειαν: May the father destroy...! opt. of wish with multiple subjects. Ὀλύμπου τοῦδε: gen. object of pple πρεσβεύω.
1390μνήμων τ᾽ Ἐρινὺς: and mindful Erinys. Δίκη: Justice, i.e. goddess of vengeance.
1390κ(αὶ ὁ) ξύναιμος: and brother; i.e. Menelaus.
1391κακούς: modifying σφε above. ὥσπερ ἤθελον: just as they wished; 3p impf. ἐθέλω.
1393ὦ...σπέρμα: O seed of...; vocative, i.e. son.
1394τάφου τοῦδε: partitive object of the infinitive. ἐᾶν: to allow you + complementary infinitive.

1396τὰ δ᾽ ἄλλα: but in respect to the rest; acc. of respect. καὶ: intensive, emphasizing the verb. ξύμπρασσε: sg. imperative. καὶ εἴ: and if...
1396τ(ὰ) ἄλλα πάντα: acc. object; i.e. other things pertaining to the burial.

1409παῖ: boy; Ajax’s son, voc. direct address. πατρός: partitive gen. object of the omitted continuation. ὅσον: as much as...; inner acc.

Commentary

1411φιλότητι: with...; dat. of manner
1411πλευρὰς τάσδ(ε): these sides; i.e. his body; acc. obj. of ἐπικούφιζ(ε) and possibly acc. of respect with θιγὼν (‘on his sides’)
1411θιγὼν: aor. pple θιγγάνω + partitive gen.
1412θερμαὶ σύριγγες: Jebb suggests these are his blood vessels rather than the wound or various other openings of the body: mouth, nose, etc.
1412ἐπικούφιζ(ε): sg. imper.
1413ἄνω φυσῶσι: are blowing up; 3p pres.
1413μέλαν μένος: dark force, black might; i.e. blood; neut. acc., Ajax is still bleeding
1414ἀλλ(ὰ) ἄγε: come, come now; ἀλλά and ἄγε often grab attention before a command. πᾶς...ἀνὴρ...σούσθω, βάτω: Let every man...; 3s pres. imperative σεύω and 3s aor. imperative βαίνω; i.e. get moving.
1414φίλος: as a friend; pred. nom. within the relative clause. ὅστις...φησὶ παρεῖναι: whoever says he is present; 3s φημί and pres. inf. πάρ-ειμι.
1416τῷδ᾽ ἀνδρὶ...τῷ πάντ(α) ἀγαθῷ: for a man noble in every way; dat. of interest. ἀγαθῷ is attributive modifying ἀνδρί; πάντα is adv. acc. πονῶν: nom. pres. pple modifying πᾶς ἀνήρ.
1417κ(αὶ) οὐδενί πω λῴονι θνητῶν: and not yet for anyone better among mortals; a second dat. of interest with partitive gen.; οὐ πω modifies πονῶν.
1418Αἴαντος: than...; gen. of comparison following λῴονι. ὅτ(ε) ἦν: when he was alive; 3s impf. εἰμί. φωνῶ: I claim; parenthetical.
1419ἦ: truly, indeed. πολλά: neut. acc. object of pple and main inf., supply things. βροτοῖς...ἰδοῦσιν: for mortals after seeing; dat. of interest and dat. pl. aor. pple ὁράω. ἔστιν: it is possible; impersonal. γνῶναι: aor. inf. γιγνώσκω.
1420πρὶν ἰδεῖν: but before one sees; πρίν often governs an infinitive; aor. inf. ὁράω. οὐδεὶς (ἐστίν) μάντις: no one is a seer.
1421τῶν μελλόντων: of what will be, of the future; objective gen. modifying μάντις. ὅ τι πράξει: namely how he will fare; indirect question in apposition to τῶν μελλόντων with 3s fut. πράσσω.

Known issues in this text

Text and commentary were digitised by OCR, anchored to individual words by a neural pass, then post-processed. These are the measured artefacts of that pipeline — the commentary itself is unaltered.
